is Markdown?","","Markdown is a plain text format for writing structured documents,","based on conventions for indicating formatting in email","and usenet posts.  It was developed by John Gruber (with","help from Aaron Swartz) and released in 2004 in the form of a","[syntax description](https://daringfireball.net/projects/markdown/syntax)","and a Perl script (`Markdown.pl`) for converting Markdown to","HTML.  In the next decade, dozens of implementations were","developed in many languages.  Some extended the original","Markdown syntax with conventions for footnotes, tables, and","other document elements.  Some allowed Markdown documents to be","rendered in formats other than HTML.  Websites like Reddit,","StackOverflow, and GitHub had millions of people using Markdown.","And Markdown started to be used beyond the web, to author books,","articles, slide shows, letters, and lecture notes.","","What distinguishes Markdown from many other lightweight markup","syntaxes, which are often easier to write, is its readability.","As Gruber writes:","","\u003e The overriding design goal for Markdown's formatting syntax is","\u003e to make it as readable as possible. The idea is that a","\u003e Markdown-formatted document should be publishable as-is, as","\u003e plain text, without looking like it's been marked up with tags","\u003e or formatting instructions.","\u003e (\u003chttps://daringfireball.net/projects/markdown/\u003e)","","The point can be illustrated by comparing a sample of","[AsciiDoc](https://asciidoc.org/) with","an equivalent sample of Markdown.  Here is a sample of","AsciiDoc from the AsciiDoc manual:","","```","1. List item one.","+","List item one continued with a second paragraph followed by an","Indented block.","+",".................","$ ls *.sh","$ mv *.sh ~/tmp",".................","+","List item continued with a third paragraph.","","2. List item two continued with an open block.","+","--","This paragraph is part of the preceding list item.","","a. This list is nested and does not require explicit item","continuation.","+","This paragraph is part of the preceding list item.","","b. List item b.","","This paragraph belongs to item two of the outer list.","--","```","","And here is the equivalent in Markdown:","```","1.  List item one.","","    List item one continued with a second paragraph followed by an","    Indented block.","","        $ ls *.sh","        $ mv *.sh ~/tmp","","    List item continued with a third paragraph.","","2.  List item two continued with an open block.","","    This paragraph is part of the preceding list item.","","    1. This list is nested and does not require explicit item continuation.","","       This paragraph is part of the preceding list item.","","    2. List item b.","","    This paragraph belongs to item two of the outer list.","```","","The AsciiDoc version is, arguably, easier to write. You don't need","to worry about indentation.  But the Markdown version is much easier","to read.  The nesting of list items is apparent to the eye in the","source, not just in the processed document.","","## Why is a spec needed?","","John Gruber's [canonical description of Markdown's","syntax](https://daringfireball.net/projects/markdown/syntax)","does not specify the syntax unambiguously.  Here are some examples of","questions it does not answer:","","1.  How much indentation is needed for a sublist?  The spec says that","    continuation paragraphs need to be indented four spaces, but is","    not fully explicit about sublists.  It is natural to think that","    they, too, must be indented four spaces, but `Markdown.pl` does","    not require that.  This is hardly a \"corner case,\" and divergences","    between implementations on this issue often lead to surprises for","    users in real documents. (See [this comment by John","    Gruber](https://web.archive.org/web/20170611172104/http://article.gmane.org/gmane.text.markdown.general/1997).)","","2.  Is a blank line needed before a block quote or heading?","    Most implementations do not require the blank line.  However,","    this can lead to unexpected results in hard-wrapped text, and","    also to ambiguities in parsing (note that some implementations","    put the heading inside the blockquote, while others do not).","    (John Gruber has also spoken [in favor of requiring the blank","    lines](https://web.archive.org/web/20170611172104/http://article.gmane.org/gmane.text.markdown.general/2146).)","","3.  Is a blank line needed before an indented code block?","    (`Markdown.pl` requires it, but this is not mentioned in the","    documentation, and some implementations do not require it.)","","    ``` markdown","    paragraph","        code?","    ```","","4.  What is the exact rule for determining when list items get","    wrapped in `\u003cp\u003e` tags?  Can a list be partially \"loose\" and partially","    \"tight\"?  What should we do with a list like this?","","    ``` markdown","    1. one","","    2. two","    3. three","    ```","","    Or this?","","    ``` markdown","    1.  one","        - a","","        - b","    2.  two","    ```","","    (There are some relevant comments by John Gruber","    [here](https://web.archive.org/web/20170611172104/http://article.gmane.org/gmane.text.markdown.general/2554).)","","5.  Can list markers be indented?  Can ordered list markers be right-aligned?","","    ``` markdown","     8. item 1","     9. item 2","    10. item 2a","    ```","","6.  Is this one list with a thematic break in its second item,","    or two lists separated by a thematic break?","","    ``` markdown","    * a","    * * * * *","    * b","    ```","","7.  When list markers change from numbers to bullets, do we have","    two lists or one?  (The Markdown syntax description suggests two,","    but the perl scripts and many other implementations produce one.)","","    ``` markdown","    1. fee","    2. fie","    -  foe","    -  fum","    ```","","8.  What are the precedence rules for the markers of inline structure?","    For example, is the following a valid link, or does the code span","    take precedence ?","","    ``` markdown","    [a backtick (`)](/url) and [another backtick (`)](/url).","    ```","","9.  What are the precedence rules for markers of emphasis and strong","    emphasis?  For example, how should the following be parsed?","","    ``` markdown","    *foo *bar* baz*","    ```","","10. What are the precedence rules between block-level and inline-level","    structure?  For example, how should the following be parsed?","","    ``` markdown","    - `a long code span can contain a hyphen like this","      - and it can screw things up`","    ```","","11. Can list items include section headings?  (`Markdown.pl` does not","    allow this, but does allow blockquotes to include headings.)","","    ``` markdown","    - # Heading","    ```","","12. Can list items be empty?","","    ``` markdown","    * a","    *","    * b","    ```","","13. Can link references be defined inside block quotes or list items?","","    ``` markdown","    \u003e Blockquote [foo].","    \u003e","    \u003e [foo]: /url","    ```","","14. If there are multiple definitions for the same reference, which takes","    precedence?","","    ``` markdown","    [foo]: /url1","    [foo]: /url2","","    [foo][]","    ```","","In the absence of a spec, early implementers consulted `Markdown.pl`","to resolve these ambiguities.  But `Markdown.pl` was quite buggy, and","gave manifestly bad results in many cases, so it was not a","satisfactory replacement for a spec.","","Because there is no unambiguous spec, implementations have diverged","considerably.  As a result, users are often surprised to find that","a document that renders one way on one system (say, a GitHub wiki)","renders differently on another (say, converting to docbook using","pandoc).  To make matters worse, because nothing in Markdown counts","as a \"syntax error,\" the divergence often isn't discovered right away.","","## About this document","","This document attempts to specify Markdown syntax unambiguously.","It contains many examples with side-by-side Markdown and","HTML.  These are intended to double as conformance tests.  An","accompanying script `spec_tests.py` can be used to run the tests","against any Markdown program:","","    python test/spec_tests.py --spec spec.txt --program PROGRAM","","Since this document describes how Markdown is to be parsed into","an abstract syntax tree, it would have made sense to use an abstract","representation of the syntax tree instead of HTML.  But HTML is capable","of representing the structural distinctions we need to make, and the","choice of HTML for the tests makes it possible to run the tests against","an implementation without writing an abstract syntax tree renderer.","","Note that not every feature of the HTML samples is mandated by","the spec.  For example, the spec says what counts as a link","destination, but it doesn't mandate that non-ASCII characters in","the URL be percent-encoded.  To use the automatic tests,","implementers will need to provide a renderer that conforms to","the expectations of the spec examples (percent-encoding","non-ASCII characters in URLs).  But a conforming implementation","can use a different renderer and may choose not to","percent-encode non-ASCII characters in URLs.","","This document is generated from a text file, `spec.txt`, written","in Markdown with a small extension for the side-by-side tests.","The script `tools/makespec.py` can be used to convert `spec.txt` into","HTML or CommonMark (which can then be converted into other formats).","","In the examples, the `→` character is used to represent tabs.","","# Preliminaries","","## Characters and lines","","Any sequence of [characters] is a valid CommonMark","document.","","A [character](@) is a Unicode code point.  Although some","code points (for example, combining accents) do not correspond to","characters in an intuitive sense, all code points count as characters","for purposes of this spec.","","This spec does not specify an encoding; it thinks of lines as composed","of [characters] rather than bytes.  A conforming parser may be limited","to a certain encoding.","","A [line](@) is a sequence of zero or more [characters]","other than line feed (`U+000A`) or carriage return (`U+000D`),","followed by a [line ending] or by the end of file.","","A [line ending](@) is a line feed (`U+000A`), a carriage return","(`U+000D`) not followed by a line feed, or a carriage return and a","following line feed.","","A line containing no characters, or a line containing only spaces","(`U+0020`) or tabs (`U+0009`), is called a [blank line](@).","","The following definitions of character classes will be used in this spec:","","A [Unicode whitespace character](@) is a character in the Unicode `Zs` general","category, or a tab (`U+0009`), line feed (`U+000A`), form feed (`U+000C`), or","carriage return (`U+000D`).","","[Unicode whitespace](@) is a sequence of one or more","[Unicode whitespace characters].","","A [tab](@) is `U+0009`.","","A [space](@) is `U+0020`.","","An [ASCII control character](@) is a character between `U+0000–1F` (both","including) or `U+007F`.","","An [ASCII punctuation character](@)","is `!`, `\"`, `#`, `$`, `%`, `\u0026`, `'`, `(`, `)`,","`*`, `+`, `,`, `-`, `.`, `/` (U+0021–2F), ","`:`, `;`, `\u003c`, `=`, `\u003e`, `?`, `@` (U+003A–0040),","`[`, `\\`, `]`, `^`, `_`, `` ` `` (U+005B–0060), ","`{`, `|`, `}`, or `~` (U+007B–007E).","","A [Unicode punctuation character](@) is a character in the Unicode `P`","(puncuation) or `S` (symbol) general categories.","","## Tabs","","Tabs in lines are not expanded to [spaces].  However,","in contexts where spaces help to define block structure,","tabs behave as if they were replaced by spaces with a tab stop","of 4 characters.","","Thus, for example, a tab can be used instead of four spaces","in an indented code block.  (Note, however, that internal","tabs are passed through as literal tabs, not expanded to","spaces.)","","```````````````````````````````` example","→foo→baz→→bim",".","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003efoo→baz→→bim","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","```````````````````````````````` example","  →foo→baz→→bim",".","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003efoo→baz→→bim","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","```````````````````````````````` example","    a→a","    ὐ→a",".","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003ea→a","ὐ→a","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","In the following example, a continuation paragraph of a list","item is indented with a tab; this has exactly the same effect","as indentation with four spaces would:","","```````````````````````````````` example","  - foo","","→bar",".","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cp\u003efoo\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cp\u003ebar\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","```````````````````````````````` example","- foo","","→→bar",".","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cp\u003efoo\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003e  bar","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","Normally the `\u003e` that begins a block quote may be followed","optionally by a space, which is not considered part of the","content.  In the following case `\u003e` is followed by a tab,","which is treated as if it were expanded into three spaces.","Since one of these spaces is considered part of the","delimiter, `foo` is considered to be indented six spaces","inside the block quote context, so we get an indented","code block starting with two spaces.","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003e→→foo",".","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003e  foo","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","```````````````````````````````` example","-→→foo",".","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003e  foo","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","    foo","→bar",".","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003efoo","bar","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","```````````````````````````````` example"," - foo","   - bar","→ - baz",".","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003efoo","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003ebar","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003ebaz\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","```````````````````````````````` example","#→Foo",".","\u003ch1\u003eFoo\u003c/h1\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","```````````````````````````````` example","*→*→*→",".","\u003chr /\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","## Insecure characters","","For security reasons, the Unicode character `U+0000` must be replaced","with the REPLACEMENT CHARACTER (`U+FFFD`).","","","## Backslash escapes","","Any ASCII punctuation character may be backslash-escaped:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\\!\\\"\\#\\$\\%\\\u0026\\'\\(\\)\\*\\+\\,\\-\\.\\/\\:\\;\\\u003c\\=\\\u003e\\?\\@\\[\\\\\\]\\^\\_\\`\\{\\|\\}\\~",".","\u003cp\u003e!\u0026quot;#$%\u0026amp;'()*+,-./:;\u0026lt;=\u0026gt;?@[\\]^_`{|}~\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Backslashes before other characters are treated as literal","backslashes:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\\→\\A\\a\\ \\3\\φ\\«",".","\u003cp\u003e\\→\\A\\a\\ \\3\\φ\\«\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Escaped characters are treated as regular characters and do","not have their usual Markdown meanings:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\\*not emphasized*","\\\u003cbr/\u003e not a tag","\\[not a link](/foo)","\\`not code`","1\\. not a list","\\* not a list","\\# not a heading","\\[foo]: /url \"not a reference\"","\\\u0026ouml; not a character entity",".","\u003cp\u003e*not emphasized*","\u0026lt;br/\u0026gt; not a tag","[not a link](/foo)","`not code`","1. not a list","* not a list","# not a heading","[foo]: /url \u0026quot;not a reference\u0026quot;","\u0026amp;ouml; not a character entity\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","If a backslash is itself escaped, the following character is not:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\\\\*emphasis*",".","\u003cp\u003e\\\u003cem\u003eemphasis\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","A backslash at the end of the line is a [hard line break]:","","```````````````````````````````` example","foo\\","bar",".","\u003cp\u003efoo\u003cbr /\u003e","bar\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Backslash escapes do not work in code blocks, code spans, autolinks, or","raw HTML:","","```````````````````````````````` example","`` \\[\\` ``",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\\[\\`\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","    \\[\\]",".","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\\[\\]","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","~~~","\\[\\]","~~~",".","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\\[\\]","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003chttps://example.com?find=\\*\u003e",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"https://example.com?find=%5C*\"\u003ehttps://example.com?find=\\*\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003ca href=\"/bar\\/)\"\u003e",".","\u003ca href=\"/bar\\/)\"\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","But they work in all other contexts, including URLs and link titles,","link references, and [info strings] in [fenced code blocks]:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo](/bar\\* \"ti\\*tle\")",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"/bar*\" title=\"ti*tle\"\u003efoo\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo]","","[foo]: /bar\\* \"ti\\*tle\"",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"/bar*\" title=\"ti*tle\"\u003efoo\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","``` foo\\+bar","foo","```",".","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-foo+bar\"\u003efoo","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","## Entity and numeric character references","","Valid HTML entity references and numeric character references","can be used in place of the corresponding Unicode character,","with the following exceptions:","","- Entity and character references are not recognized in code","  blocks and code spans.","","- Entity and character references cannot stand in place of","  special characters that define structural elements in","  CommonMark.  For example, although `\u0026#42;` can be used","  in place of a literal `*` character, `\u0026#42;` cannot replace","  `*` in emphasis delimiters, bullet list markers, or thematic","  breaks.","","Conforming CommonMark parsers need not store information about","whether a particular character was represented in the source","using a Unicode character or an entity reference.","","[Entity references](@) consist of `\u0026` + any of the valid","HTML5 entity names + `;`. The","document \u003chttps://html.spec.whatwg.org/entities.json\u003e","is used as an authoritative source for the valid entity","references and their corresponding code points.","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u0026nbsp; \u0026amp; \u0026copy; \u0026AElig; \u0026Dcaron;","\u0026frac34; \u0026HilbertSpace; \u0026DifferentialD;","\u0026ClockwiseContourIntegral; \u0026ngE;",".","\u003cp\u003e  \u0026amp; © Æ Ď","¾ ℋ ⅆ","∲ ≧̸\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","[Decimal numeric character","references](@)","consist of `\u0026#` + a string of 1--7 arabic digits + `;`. A","numeric character reference is parsed as the corresponding","Unicode character. Invalid Unicode code points will be replaced by","the REPLACEMENT CHARACTER (`U+FFFD`).  For security reasons,","the code point `U+0000` will also be replaced by `U+FFFD`.","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u0026#35; \u0026#1234; \u0026#992; \u0026#0;",".","\u003cp\u003e# Ӓ Ϡ �\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","[Hexadecimal numeric character","references](@) consist of `\u0026#` +","either `X` or `x` + a string of 1-6 hexadecimal digits + `;`.","They too are parsed as the corresponding Unicode character (this","time specified with a hexadecimal numeral instead of decimal).","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u0026#X22; \u0026#XD06; \u0026#xcab;",".","\u003cp\u003e\u0026quot; ആ ಫ\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Here are some nonentities:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u0026nbsp \u0026x; \u0026#; \u0026#x;","\u0026#87654321;","\u0026#abcdef0;","\u0026ThisIsNotDefined; \u0026hi?;",".","\u003cp\u003e\u0026amp;nbsp \u0026amp;x; \u0026amp;#; \u0026amp;#x;","\u0026amp;#87654321;","\u0026amp;#abcdef0;","\u0026amp;ThisIsNotDefined; \u0026amp;hi?;\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Although HTML5 does accept some entity references","without a trailing semicolon (such as `\u0026copy`), these are not","recognized here, because it makes the grammar too ambiguous:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u0026copy",".","\u003cp\u003e\u0026amp;copy\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Strings that are not on the list of HTML5 named entities are not","recognized as entity references either:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u0026MadeUpEntity;",".","\u003cp\u003e\u0026amp;MadeUpEntity;\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Entity and numeric character references are recognized in any","context besides code spans or code blocks, including","URLs, [link titles], and [fenced code block][] [info strings]:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003ca href=\"\u0026ouml;\u0026ouml;.html\"\u003e",".","\u003ca href=\"\u0026ouml;\u0026ouml;.html\"\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo](/f\u0026ouml;\u0026ouml; \"f\u0026ouml;\u0026ouml;\")",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"/f%C3%B6%C3%B6\" title=\"föö\"\u003efoo\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo]","","[foo]: /f\u0026ouml;\u0026ouml; \"f\u0026ouml;\u0026ouml;\"",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"/f%C3%B6%C3%B6\" title=\"föö\"\u003efoo\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","``` f\u0026ouml;\u0026ouml;","foo","```",".","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-föö\"\u003efoo","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Entity and numeric character references are treated as literal","text in code spans and code blocks:","","```````````````````````````````` example","`f\u0026ouml;\u0026ouml;`",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ccode\u003ef\u0026amp;ouml;\u0026amp;ouml;\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","    f\u0026ouml;f\u0026ouml;",".","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003ef\u0026amp;ouml;f\u0026amp;ouml;","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Entity and numeric character references cannot be used","in place of symbols indicating structure in CommonMark","documents.","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u0026#42;foo\u0026#42;","*foo*",".","\u003cp\u003e*foo*","\u003cem\u003efoo\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u0026#42; foo","","* foo",".","\u003cp\u003e* foo\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003efoo\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","```````````````````````````````` example","foo\u0026#10;\u0026#10;bar",".","\u003cp\u003efoo","","bar\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u0026#9;foo",".","\u003cp\u003e→foo\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","[a](url \u0026quot;tit\u0026quot;)",".","\u003cp\u003e[a](url \u0026quot;tit\u0026quot;)\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","","# Blocks and inlines","","We can think of a document as a sequence of","[blocks](@)---structural elements like paragraphs, block","quotations, lists, headings, rules, and code blocks.  Some blocks (like","block quotes and list items) contain other blocks; others (like","headings and paragraphs) contain [inline](@) content---text,","links, emphasized text, images, code spans, and so on.","","## Precedence","","Indicators of block structure always take precedence over indicators","of inline structure.  So, for example, the following is a list with","two items, not a list with one item containing a code span:","","```````````````````````````````` example","- `one","- two`",".","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003e`one\u003c/li\u003e","\u003cli\u003etwo`\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","This means that parsing can proceed in two steps:  first, the block","structure of the document can be discerned; second, text lines inside","paragraphs, headings, and other block constructs can be parsed for inline","structure.  The second step requires information about link reference","definitions that will be available only at the end of the first","step.  Note that the first step requires processing lines in sequence,","but the second can be parallelized, since the inline parsing of","one block element does not affect the inline parsing of any other.","","## Container blocks and leaf blocks","","We can divide blocks into two types:","[container blocks](#container-blocks),","which can contain other blocks, and [leaf blocks](#leaf-blocks),","which cannot.","","# Leaf blocks","","This section describes the different kinds of leaf block that make up a","Markdown document.","","## Thematic breaks","","A line consisting of optionally up to three spaces of indentation, followed by a","sequence of three or more matching `-`, `_`, or `*` characters, each followed","optionally by any number of spaces or tabs, forms a","[thematic break](@).","","```````````````````````````````` example","***","---","___",".","\u003chr /\u003e","\u003chr /\u003e","\u003chr /\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Wrong characters:","","```````````````````````````````` example","+++",".","\u003cp\u003e+++\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","===",".","\u003cp\u003e===\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Not enough characters:","","```````````````````````````````` example","--","**","__",".","\u003cp\u003e--","**","__\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Up to three spaces of indentation are allowed:","","```````````````````````````````` example"," ***","  ***","   ***",".","\u003chr /\u003e","\u003chr /\u003e","\u003chr /\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Four spaces of indentation is too many:","","```````````````````````````````` example","    ***",".","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003e***","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","Foo","    ***",".","\u003cp\u003eFoo","***\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","More than three characters may be used:","","```````````````````````````````` example","_____________________________________",".","\u003chr /\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Spaces and tabs are allowed between the characters:","","```````````````````````````````` example"," - - -",".","\u003chr /\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example"," **  * ** * ** * **",".","\u003chr /\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","-     -      -      -",".","\u003chr /\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Spaces and tabs are allowed at the end:","","```````````````````````````````` example","- - - -    ",".","\u003chr /\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","However, no other characters may occur in the line:","","```````````````````````````````` example","_ _ _ _ a","","a------","","---a---",".","\u003cp\u003e_ _ _ _ a\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cp\u003ea------\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cp\u003e---a---\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","It is required that all of the characters other than spaces or tabs be the same.","So, this is not a thematic break:","","```````````````````````````````` example"," *-*",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cem\u003e-\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Thematic breaks do not need blank lines before or after:","","```````````````````````````````` example","- foo","***","- bar",".","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003efoo\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","\u003chr /\u003e","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003ebar\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Thematic breaks can interrupt a paragraph:","","```````````````````````````````` example","Foo","***","bar",".","\u003cp\u003eFoo\u003c/p\u003e","\u003chr /\u003e","\u003cp\u003ebar\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","If a line of dashes that meets the above conditions for being a","thematic break could also be interpreted as the underline of a [setext","heading], the interpretation as a","[setext heading] takes precedence. Thus, for example,","this is a setext heading, not a paragraph followed by a thematic break:","","```````````````````````````````` example","Foo","---","bar",".","\u003ch2\u003eFoo\u003c/h2\u003e","\u003cp\u003ebar\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","When both a thematic break and a list item are possible","interpretations of a line, the thematic break takes precedence:","","```````````````````````````````` example","* Foo","* * *","* Bar",".","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003eFoo\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","\u003chr /\u003e","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003eBar\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","If you want a thematic break in a list item, use a different bullet:","","```````````````````````````````` example","- Foo","- * * *",".","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003eFoo\u003c/li\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003chr /\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","## ATX headings","","An [ATX heading](@)","consists of a string of characters, parsed as inline content, between an","opening sequence of 1--6 unescaped `#` characters and an optional","closing sequence of any number of unescaped `#` characters.","The opening sequence of `#` characters must be followed by spaces or tabs, or","by the end of line. The optional closing sequence of `#`s must be preceded by","spaces or tabs and may be followed by spaces or tabs only.  The opening","`#` character may be preceded by up to three spaces of indentation.  The raw","contents of the heading are stripped of leading and trailing space or tabs","before being parsed as inline content.  The heading level is equal to the number","of `#` characters in the opening sequence.","","Simple headings:","","```````````````````````````````` example","# foo","## foo","### foo","#### foo","##### foo","###### foo",".","\u003ch1\u003efoo\u003c/h1\u003e","\u003ch2\u003efoo\u003c/h2\u003e","\u003ch3\u003efoo\u003c/h3\u003e","\u003ch4\u003efoo\u003c/h4\u003e","\u003ch5\u003efoo\u003c/h5\u003e","\u003ch6\u003efoo\u003c/h6\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","More than six `#` characters is not a heading:","","```````````````````````````````` example","####### foo",".","\u003cp\u003e####### foo\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","At least one space or tab is required between the `#` characters and the","heading's contents, unless the heading is empty.  Note that many","implementations currently do not require the space.  However, the","space was required by the","[original ATX implementation](http://www.aaronsw.com/2002/atx/atx.py),","and it helps prevent things like the following from being parsed as","headings:","","```````````````````````````````` example","#5 bolt","","#hashtag",".","\u003cp\u003e#5 bolt\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cp\u003e#hashtag\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","This is not a heading, because the first `#` is escaped:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\\## foo",".","\u003cp\u003e## foo\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Contents are parsed as inlines:","","```````````````````````````````` example","# foo *bar* \\*baz\\*",".","\u003ch1\u003efoo \u003cem\u003ebar\u003c/em\u003e *baz*\u003c/h1\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Leading and trailing spaces or tabs are ignored in parsing inline content:","","```````````````````````````````` example","#                  foo                     ",".","\u003ch1\u003efoo\u003c/h1\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Up to three spaces of indentation are allowed:","","```````````````````````````````` example"," ### foo","  ## foo","   # foo",".","\u003ch3\u003efoo\u003c/h3\u003e","\u003ch2\u003efoo\u003c/h2\u003e","\u003ch1\u003efoo\u003c/h1\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Four spaces of indentation is too many:","","```````````````````````````````` example","    # foo",".","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003e# foo","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","foo","    # bar",".","\u003cp\u003efoo","# bar\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","A closing sequence of `#` characters is optional:","","```````````````````````````````` example","## foo ##","  ###   bar    ###",".","\u003ch2\u003efoo\u003c/h2\u003e","\u003ch3\u003ebar\u003c/h3\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","It need not be the same length as the opening sequence:","","```````````````````````````````` example","# foo ##################################","##### foo ##",".","\u003ch1\u003efoo\u003c/h1\u003e","\u003ch5\u003efoo\u003c/h5\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Spaces or tabs are allowed after the closing sequence:","","```````````````````````````````` example","### foo ###     ",".","\u003ch3\u003efoo\u003c/h3\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","A sequence of `#` characters with anything but spaces or tabs following it","is not a closing sequence, but counts as part of the contents of the","heading:","","```````````````````````````````` example","### foo ### b",".","\u003ch3\u003efoo ### b\u003c/h3\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","The closing sequence must be preceded by a space or tab:","","```````````````````````````````` example","# foo#",".","\u003ch1\u003efoo#\u003c/h1\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Backslash-escaped `#` characters do not count as part","of the closing sequence:","","```````````````````````````````` example","### foo \\###","## foo #\\##","# foo \\#",".","\u003ch3\u003efoo ###\u003c/h3\u003e","\u003ch2\u003efoo ###\u003c/h2\u003e","\u003ch1\u003efoo #\u003c/h1\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","ATX headings need not be separated from surrounding content by blank","lines, and they can interrupt paragraphs:","","```````````````````````````````` example","****","## foo","****",".","\u003chr /\u003e","\u003ch2\u003efoo\u003c/h2\u003e","\u003chr /\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","Foo bar","# baz","Bar foo",".","\u003cp\u003eFoo bar\u003c/p\u003e","\u003ch1\u003ebaz\u003c/h1\u003e","\u003cp\u003eBar foo\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","ATX headings can be empty:","","```````````````````````````````` example","## ","#","### ###",".","\u003ch2\u003e\u003c/h2\u003e","\u003ch1\u003e\u003c/h1\u003e","\u003ch3\u003e\u003c/h3\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","## Setext headings","","A [setext heading](@) consists of one or more","lines of text, not interrupted by a blank line, of which the first line does not","have more than 3 spaces of indentation, followed by","a [setext heading underline].  The lines of text must be such","that, were they not followed by the setext heading underline,","they would be interpreted as a paragraph:  they cannot be","interpretable as a [code fence], [ATX heading][ATX headings],","[block quote][block quotes], [thematic break][thematic breaks],","[list item][list items], or [HTML block][HTML blocks].","","A [setext heading underline](@) is a sequence of","`=` characters or a sequence of `-` characters, with no more than 3","spaces of indentation and any number of trailing spaces or tabs.","","The heading is a level 1 heading if `=` characters are used in","the [setext heading underline], and a level 2 heading if `-`","characters are used.  The contents of the heading are the result","of parsing the preceding lines of text as CommonMark inline","content.","","In general, a setext heading need not be preceded or followed by a","blank line.  However, it cannot interrupt a paragraph, so when a","setext heading comes after a paragraph, a blank line is needed between","them.","","Simple examples:","","```````````````````````````````` example","Foo *bar*","=========","","Foo *bar*","---------",".","\u003ch1\u003eFoo \u003cem\u003ebar\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/h1\u003e","\u003ch2\u003eFoo \u003cem\u003ebar\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/h2\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","The content of the header may span more than one line:","","```````````````````````````````` example","Foo *bar","baz*","====",".","\u003ch1\u003eFoo \u003cem\u003ebar","baz\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/h1\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","The contents are the result of parsing the headings's raw","content as inlines.  The heading's raw content is formed by","concatenating the lines and removing initial and final","spaces or tabs.","","```````````````````````````````` example","  Foo *bar","baz*→","====",".","\u003ch1\u003eFoo \u003cem\u003ebar","baz\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/h1\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","The underlining can be any length:","","```````````````````````````````` example","Foo","-------------------------","","Foo","=",".","\u003ch2\u003eFoo\u003c/h2\u003e","\u003ch1\u003eFoo\u003c/h1\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","The heading content can be preceded by up to three spaces of indentation, and","need not line up with the underlining:","","```````````````````````````````` example","   Foo","---","","  Foo","-----","","  Foo","  ===",".","\u003ch2\u003eFoo\u003c/h2\u003e","\u003ch2\u003eFoo\u003c/h2\u003e","\u003ch1\u003eFoo\u003c/h1\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Four spaces of indentation is too many:","","```````````````````````````````` example","    Foo","    ---","","    Foo","---",".","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003eFoo","---","","Foo","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","\u003chr /\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","The setext heading underline can be preceded by up to three spaces of","indentation, and may have trailing spaces or tabs:","","```````````````````````````````` example","Foo","   ----      ",".","\u003ch2\u003eFoo\u003c/h2\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Four spaces of indentation is too many:","","```````````````````````````````` example","Foo","    ---",".","\u003cp\u003eFoo","---\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","The setext heading underline cannot contain internal spaces or tabs:","","```````````````````````````````` example","Foo","= =","","Foo","--- -",".","\u003cp\u003eFoo","= =\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cp\u003eFoo\u003c/p\u003e","\u003chr /\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Trailing spaces or tabs in the content line do not cause a hard line break:","","```````````````````````````````` example","Foo  ","-----",".","\u003ch2\u003eFoo\u003c/h2\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Nor does a backslash at the end:","","```````````````````````````````` example","Foo\\","----",".","\u003ch2\u003eFoo\\\u003c/h2\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Since indicators of block structure take precedence over","indicators of inline structure, the following are setext headings:","","```````````````````````````````` example","`Foo","----","`","","\u003ca title=\"a lot","---","of dashes\"/\u003e",".","\u003ch2\u003e`Foo\u003c/h2\u003e","\u003cp\u003e`\u003c/p\u003e","\u003ch2\u003e\u0026lt;a title=\u0026quot;a lot\u003c/h2\u003e","\u003cp\u003eof dashes\u0026quot;/\u0026gt;\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","The setext heading underline cannot be a [lazy continuation","line] in a list item or block quote:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003e Foo","---",".","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003cp\u003eFoo\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","\u003chr /\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003e foo","bar","===",".","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003cp\u003efoo","bar","===\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","- Foo","---",".","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003eFoo\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","\u003chr /\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","A blank line is needed between a paragraph and a following","setext heading, since otherwise the paragraph becomes part","of the heading's content:","","```````````````````````````````` example","Foo","Bar","---",".","\u003ch2\u003eFoo","Bar\u003c/h2\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","But in general a blank line is not required before or after","setext headings:","","```````````````````````````````` example","---","Foo","---","Bar","---","Baz",".","\u003chr /\u003e","\u003ch2\u003eFoo\u003c/h2\u003e","\u003ch2\u003eBar\u003c/h2\u003e","\u003cp\u003eBaz\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Setext headings cannot be empty:","","```````````````````````````````` example","","====",".","\u003cp\u003e====\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Setext heading text lines must not be interpretable as block","constructs other than paragraphs.  So, the line of dashes","in these examples gets interpreted as a thematic break:","","```````````````````````````````` example","---","---",".","\u003chr /\u003e","\u003chr /\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","- foo","-----",".","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003efoo\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","\u003chr /\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","    foo","---",".","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003efoo","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","\u003chr /\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003e foo","-----",".","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003cp\u003efoo\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","\u003chr /\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","If you want a heading with `\u003e foo` as its literal text, you can","use backslash escapes:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\\\u003e foo","------",".","\u003ch2\u003e\u0026gt; foo\u003c/h2\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","**Compatibility note:**  Most existing Markdown implementations","do not allow the text of setext headings to span multiple lines.","But there is no consensus about how to interpret","","``` markdown","Foo","bar","---","baz","```","","One can find four different interpretations:","","1. paragraph \"Foo\", heading \"bar\", paragraph \"baz\"","2. paragraph \"Foo bar\", thematic break, paragraph \"baz\"","3. paragraph \"Foo bar --- baz\"","4. heading \"Foo bar\", paragraph \"baz\"","","We find interpretation 4 most natural, and interpretation 4","increases the expressive power of CommonMark, by allowing","multiline headings.  Authors who want interpretation 1 can","put a blank line after the first paragraph:","","```````````````````````````````` example","Foo","","bar","---","baz",".","\u003cp\u003eFoo\u003c/p\u003e","\u003ch2\u003ebar\u003c/h2\u003e","\u003cp\u003ebaz\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Authors who want interpretation 2 can put blank lines around","the thematic break,","","```````````````````````````````` example","Foo","bar","","---","","baz",".","\u003cp\u003eFoo","bar\u003c/p\u003e","\u003chr /\u003e","\u003cp\u003ebaz\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","or use a thematic break that cannot count as a [setext heading","underline], such as","","```````````````````````````````` example","Foo","bar","* * *","baz",".","\u003cp\u003eFoo","bar\u003c/p\u003e","\u003chr /\u003e","\u003cp\u003ebaz\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Authors who want interpretation 3 can use backslash escapes:","","```````````````````````````````` example","Foo","bar","\\---","baz",".","\u003cp\u003eFoo","bar","---","baz\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","## Indented code blocks","","An [indented code block](@) is composed of one or more","[indented chunks] separated by blank lines.","An [indented chunk](@) is a sequence of non-blank lines,","each preceded by four or more spaces of indentation. The contents of the code","block are the literal contents of the lines, including trailing","[line endings], minus four spaces of indentation.","An indented code block has no [info string].","","An indented code block cannot interrupt a paragraph, so there must be","a blank line between a paragraph and a following indented code block.","(A blank line is not needed, however, between a code block and a following","paragraph.)","","```````````````````````````````` example","    a simple","      indented code block",".","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003ea simple","  indented code block","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","If there is any ambiguity between an interpretation of indentation","as a code block and as indicating that material belongs to a [list","item][list items], the list item interpretation takes precedence:","","```````````````````````````````` example","  - foo","","    bar",".","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cp\u003efoo\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cp\u003ebar\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","1.  foo","","    - bar",".","\u003col\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cp\u003efoo\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003ebar\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ol\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","","The contents of a code block are literal text, and do not get parsed","as Markdown:","","```````````````````````````````` example","    \u003ca/\u003e","    *hi*","","    - one",".","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u0026lt;a/\u0026gt;","*hi*","","- one","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Here we have three chunks separated by blank lines:","","```````````````````````````````` example","    chunk1","","    chunk2","  "," "," ","    chunk3",".","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003echunk1","","chunk2","","","","chunk3","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Any initial spaces or tabs beyond four spaces of indentation will be included in","the content, even in interior blank lines:","","```````````````````````````````` example","    chunk1","      ","      chunk2",".","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003echunk1","  ","  chunk2","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","An indented code block cannot interrupt a paragraph.  (This","allows hanging indents and the like.)","","```````````````````````````````` example","Foo","    bar","",".","\u003cp\u003eFoo","bar\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","However, any non-blank line with fewer than four spaces of indentation ends","the code block immediately.  So a paragraph may occur immediately","after indented code:","","```````````````````````````````` example","    foo","bar",".","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003efoo","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","\u003cp\u003ebar\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","And indented code can occur immediately before and after other kinds of","blocks:","","```````````````````````````````` example","# Heading","    foo","Heading","------","    foo","----",".","\u003ch1\u003eHeading\u003c/h1\u003e","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003efoo","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","\u003ch2\u003eHeading\u003c/h2\u003e","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003efoo","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","\u003chr /\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","The first line can be preceded by more than four spaces of indentation:","","```````````````````````````````` example","        foo","    bar",".","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003e    foo","bar","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Blank lines preceding or following an indented code block","are not included in it:","","```````````````````````````````` example","","    ","    foo","    ","",".","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003efoo","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Trailing spaces or tabs are included in the code block's content:","","```````````````````````````````` example","    foo  ",".","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003efoo  ","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","","## Fenced code blocks","","A [code fence](@) is a sequence","of at least three consecutive backtick characters (`` ` ``) or","tildes (`~`).  (Tildes and backticks cannot be mixed.)","A [fenced code block](@)","begins with a code fence, preceded by up to three spaces of indentation.","","The line with the opening code fence may optionally contain some text","following the code fence; this is trimmed of leading and trailing","spaces or tabs and called the [info string](@). If the [info string] comes","after a backtick fence, it may not contain any backtick","characters.  (The reason for this restriction is that otherwise","some inline code would be incorrectly interpreted as the","beginning of a fenced code block.)","","The content of the code block consists of all subsequent lines, until","a closing [code fence] of the same type as the code block","began with (backticks or tildes), and with at least as many backticks","or tildes as the opening code fence.  If the leading code fence is","preceded by N spaces of indentation, then up to N spaces of indentation are","removed from each line of the content (if present).  (If a content line is not","indented, it is preserved unchanged.  If it is indented N spaces or less, all","of the indentation is removed.)","","The closing code fence may be preceded by up to three spaces of indentation, and","may be followed only by spaces or tabs, which are ignored.  If the end of the","containing block (or document) is reached and no closing code fence","has been found, the code block contains all of the lines after the","opening code fence until the end of the containing block (or","document).  (An alternative spec would require backtracking in the","event that a closing code fence is not found.  But this makes parsing","much less efficient, and there seems to be no real downside to the","behavior described here.)","","A fenced code block may interrupt a paragraph, and does not require","a blank line either before or after.","","The content of a code fence is treated as literal text, not parsed","as inlines.  The first word of the [info string] is typically used to","specify the language of the code sample, and rendered in the `class`","attribute of the `code` tag.  However, this spec does not mandate any","particular treatment of the [info string].","","Here is a simple example with backticks:","","```````````````````````````````` example","```","\u003c"," \u003e","```",".","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u0026lt;"," \u0026gt;","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","With tildes:","","```````````````````````````````` example","~~~","\u003c"," \u003e","~~~",".","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u0026lt;"," \u0026gt;","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","Fewer than three backticks is not enough:","","```````````````````````````````` example","``","foo","``",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ccode\u003efoo\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","The closing code fence must use the same character as the opening","fence:","","```````````````````````````````` example","```","aaa","~~~","```",".","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003eaaa","~~~","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","~~~","aaa","```","~~~",".","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003eaaa","```","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","The closing code fence must be at least as long as the opening fence:","","```````````````````````````````` example","````","aaa","```","``````",".","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003eaaa","```","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","~~~~","aaa","~~~","~~~~",".","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003eaaa","~~~","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Unclosed code blocks are closed by the end of the document","(or the enclosing [block quote][block quotes] or [list item][list items]):","","```````````````````````````````` example","```",".","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","`````","","```","aaa",".","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003e","```","aaa","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003e ```","\u003e aaa","","bbb",".","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003eaaa","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","\u003cp\u003ebbb\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","A code block can have all empty lines as its content:","","```````````````````````````````` example","```","","  ","```",".","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003e","  ","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","A code block can be empty:","","```````````````````````````````` example","```","```",".","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Fences can be indented.  If the opening fence is indented,","content lines will have equivalent opening indentation removed,","if present:","","```````````````````````````````` example"," ```"," aaa","aaa","```",".","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003eaaa","aaa","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","  ```","aaa","  aaa","aaa","  ```",".","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003eaaa","aaa","aaa","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","   ```","   aaa","    aaa","  aaa","   ```",".","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003eaaa"," aaa","aaa","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Four spaces of indentation is too many:","","```````````````````````````````` example","    ```","    aaa","    ```",".","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003e```","aaa","```","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Closing fences may be preceded by up to three spaces of indentation, and their","indentation need not match that of the opening fence:","","```````````````````````````````` example","```","aaa","  ```",".","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003eaaa","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","   ```","aaa","  ```",".","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003eaaa","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","This is not a closing fence, because it is indented 4 spaces:","","```````````````````````````````` example","```","aaa","    ```",".","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003eaaa","    ```","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","","Code fences (opening and closing) cannot contain internal spaces or tabs:","","```````````````````````````````` example","``` ```","aaa",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ccode\u003e \u003c/code\u003e","aaa\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","~~~~~~","aaa","~~~ ~~",".","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003eaaa","~~~ ~~","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Fenced code blocks can interrupt paragraphs, and can be followed","directly by paragraphs, without a blank line between:","","```````````````````````````````` example","foo","```","bar","```","baz",".","\u003cp\u003efoo\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003ebar","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","\u003cp\u003ebaz\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Other blocks can also occur before and after fenced code blocks","without an intervening blank line:","","```````````````````````````````` example","foo","---","~~~","bar","~~~","# baz",".","\u003ch2\u003efoo\u003c/h2\u003e","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003ebar","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","\u003ch1\u003ebaz\u003c/h1\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","An [info string] can be provided after the opening code fence.","Although this spec doesn't mandate any particular treatment of","the info string, the first word is typically used to specify","the language of the code block. In HTML output, the language is","normally indicated by adding a class to the `code` element consisting","of `language-` followed by the language name.","","```````````````````````````````` example","```ruby","def foo(x)","  return 3","end","```",".","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-ruby\"\u003edef foo(x)","  return 3","end","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","~~~~    ruby startline=3 $%@#$","def foo(x)","  return 3","end","~~~~~~~",".","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-ruby\"\u003edef foo(x)","  return 3","end","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","````;","````",".","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-;\"\u003e\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","[Info strings] for backtick code blocks cannot contain backticks:","","```````````````````````````````` example","``` aa ```","foo",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ccode\u003eaa\u003c/code\u003e","foo\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","[Info strings] for tilde code blocks can contain backticks and tildes:","","```````````````````````````````` example","~~~ aa ``` ~~~","foo","~~~",".","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-aa\"\u003efoo","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Closing code fences cannot have [info strings]:","","```````````````````````````````` example","```","``` aaa","```",".","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003e``` aaa","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","","## HTML blocks","","An [HTML block](@) is a group of lines that is treated","as raw HTML (and will not be escaped in HTML output).","","There are seven kinds of [HTML block], which can be defined by their","start and end conditions.  The block begins with a line that meets a","[start condition](@) (after up to three optional spaces of indentation).","It ends with the first subsequent line that meets a matching","[end condition](@), or the last line of the document, or the last line of","the [container block](#container-blocks) containing the current HTML","block, if no line is encountered that meets the [end condition].  If","the first line meets both the [start condition] and the [end","condition], the block will contain just that line.","","1.  **Start condition:**  line begins with the string `\u003cpre`,","`\u003cscript`, `\u003cstyle`, or `\u003ctextarea` (case-insensitive), followed by a space,","a tab, the string `\u003e`, or the end of the line.\\","**End condition:**  line contains an end tag","`\u003c/pre\u003e`, `\u003c/script\u003e`, `\u003c/style\u003e`, or `\u003c/textarea\u003e` (case-insensitive; it","need not match the start tag).","","2.  **Start condition:** line begins with the string `\u003c!--`.\\","**End condition:**  line contains the string `--\u003e`.","","3.  **Start condition:** line begins with the string `\u003c?`.\\","**End condition:** line contains the string `?\u003e`.","","4.  **Start condition:** line begins with the string `\u003c!`","followed by an ASCII letter.\\","**End condition:** line contains the character `\u003e`.","","5.  **Start condition:**  line begins with the string","`\u003c![CDATA[`.\\","**End condition:** line contains the string `]]\u003e`.","","6.  **Start condition:** line begins with the string `\u003c` or `\u003c/`","followed by one of the strings (case-insensitive) `address`,","`article`, `aside`, `base`, `basefont`, `blockquote`, `body`,","`caption`, `center`, `col`, `colgroup`, `dd`, `details`, `dialog`,","`dir`, `div`, `dl`, `dt`, `fieldset`, `figcaption`, `figure`,","`footer`, `form`, `frame`, `frameset`,","`h1`, `h2`, `h3`, `h4`, `h5`, `h6`, `head`, `header`, `hr`,","`html`, `iframe`, `legend`, `li`, `link`, `main`, `menu`, `menuitem`,","`nav`, `noframes`, `ol`, `optgroup`, `option`, `p`, `param`,","`search`, `section`, `summary`, `table`, `tbody`, `td`,","`tfoot`, `th`, `thead`, `title`, `tr`, `track`, `ul`, followed","by a space, a tab, the end of the line, the string `\u003e`, or","the string `/\u003e`.\\","**End condition:** line is followed by a [blank line].","","7.  **Start condition:**  line begins with a complete [open tag]","(with any [tag name] other than `pre`, `script`,","`style`, or `textarea`) or a complete [closing tag],","all on a single line, followed by zero or more spaces and tabs,","followed by the end of the line.\\","**End condition:** line is followed by a [blank line].","","HTML blocks continue until they are closed by their appropriate","[end condition], or the last line of the document or other [container","block](#container-blocks).  This means any HTML **within an HTML","block** that might otherwise be recognised as a start condition will","be ignored by the parser and passed through as-is, without changing","the parser's state.","","For instance, `\u003cpre\u003e` within an HTML block started by `\u003ctable\u003e` will not affect","the parser state; as the HTML block was started in by start condition 6, it","will end at any blank line. This can be surprising:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003ctable\u003e\u003ctr\u003e\u003ctd\u003e","\u003cpre\u003e","**Hello**,","","_world_.","\u003c/pre\u003e","\u003c/td\u003e\u003c/tr\u003e\u003c/table\u003e",".","\u003ctable\u003e\u003ctr\u003e\u003ctd\u003e","\u003cpre\u003e","**Hello**,","\u003cp\u003e\u003cem\u003eworld\u003c/em\u003e.","\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/td\u003e\u003c/tr\u003e\u003c/table\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","In this case, the HTML block is terminated by the blank line — the `**Hello**`","text remains verbatim — and regular parsing resumes, with a paragraph,","emphasised `world` and inline and block HTML following.","","All types of [HTML blocks] except type 7 may interrupt","a paragraph.  Blocks of type 7 may not interrupt a paragraph.","(This restriction is intended to prevent unwanted interpretation","of long tags inside a wrapped paragraph as starting HTML blocks.)","","Some simple examples follow.  Here are some basic HTML blocks","of type 6:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003ctable\u003e","  \u003ctr\u003e","    \u003ctd\u003e","           hi","    \u003c/td\u003e","  \u003c/tr\u003e","\u003c/table\u003e","","okay.",".","\u003ctable\u003e","  \u003ctr\u003e","    \u003ctd\u003e","           hi","    \u003c/td\u003e","  \u003c/tr\u003e","\u003c/table\u003e","\u003cp\u003eokay.\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example"," \u003cdiv\u003e","  *hello*","         \u003cfoo\u003e\u003ca\u003e","."," \u003cdiv\u003e","  *hello*","         \u003cfoo\u003e\u003ca\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","A block can also start with a closing tag:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003c/div\u003e","*foo*",".","\u003c/div\u003e","*foo*","````````````````````````````````","","","Here we have two HTML blocks with a Markdown paragraph between them:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003cDIV CLASS=\"foo\"\u003e","","*Markdown*","","\u003c/DIV\u003e",".","\u003cDIV CLASS=\"foo\"\u003e","\u003cp\u003e\u003cem\u003eMarkdown\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/DIV\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","The tag on the first line can be partial, as long","as it is split where there would be whitespace:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003cdiv id=\"foo\"","  class=\"bar\"\u003e","\u003c/div\u003e",".","\u003cdiv id=\"foo\"","  class=\"bar\"\u003e","\u003c/div\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003cdiv id=\"foo\" class=\"bar","  baz\"\u003e","\u003c/div\u003e",".","\u003cdiv id=\"foo\" class=\"bar","  baz\"\u003e","\u003c/div\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","An open tag need not be closed:","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003cdiv\u003e","*foo*","","*bar*",".","\u003cdiv\u003e","*foo*","\u003cp\u003e\u003cem\u003ebar\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","","A partial tag need not even be completed (garbage","in, garbage out):","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003cdiv id=\"foo\"","*hi*",".","\u003cdiv id=\"foo\"","*hi*","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003cdiv class","foo",".","\u003cdiv class","foo","````````````````````````````````","","","The initial tag doesn't even need to be a valid","tag, as long as it starts like one:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003cdiv *???-\u0026\u0026\u0026-\u003c---","*foo*",".","\u003cdiv *???-\u0026\u0026\u0026-\u003c---","*foo*","````````````````````````````````","","","In type 6 blocks, the initial tag need not be on a line by","itself:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003cdiv\u003e\u003ca href=\"bar\"\u003e*foo*\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e",".","\u003cdiv\u003e\u003ca href=\"bar\"\u003e*foo*\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003ctable\u003e\u003ctr\u003e\u003ctd\u003e","foo","\u003c/td\u003e\u003c/tr\u003e\u003c/table\u003e",".","\u003ctable\u003e\u003ctr\u003e\u003ctd\u003e","foo","\u003c/td\u003e\u003c/tr\u003e\u003c/table\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Everything until the next blank line or end of document","gets included in the HTML block.  So, in the following","examples, what looks like a Markdown code block or block quote","is actually part of the HTML block, which continues until a blank","line or the end of the document is reached:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003cdiv\u003e\u003c/div\u003e","``` c","int x = 33;","```",".","\u003cdiv\u003e\u003c/div\u003e","``` c","int x = 33;","```","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003cdiv","\u003e not quoted text",".","\u003cdiv","\u003e not quoted text","````````````````````````````````","","","To start an [HTML block] with a tag that is *not* in the","list of block-level tags in (6), you must put the tag by","itself on the first line (and it must be complete):","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003ca href=\"foo\"\u003e","*bar*","\u003c/a\u003e",".","\u003ca href=\"foo\"\u003e","*bar*","\u003c/a\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","In type 7 blocks, the [tag name] can be anything:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003cWarning\u003e","*bar*","\u003c/Warning\u003e",".","\u003cWarning\u003e","*bar*","\u003c/Warning\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003ci class=\"foo\"\u003e","*bar*","\u003c/i\u003e",".","\u003ci class=\"foo\"\u003e","*bar*","\u003c/i\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003c/ins\u003e","*bar*",".","\u003c/ins\u003e","*bar*","````````````````````````````````","","","These rules are designed to allow us to work with tags that","can function as either block-level or inline-level tags.","The `\u003cdel\u003e` tag is a nice example.  We can surround content with","`\u003cdel\u003e` tags in three different ways.  In this case, we get a raw","HTML block, because the `\u003cdel\u003e` tag is on a line by itself:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003cdel\u003e","*foo*","\u003c/del\u003e",".","\u003cdel\u003e","*foo*","\u003c/del\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","In this case, we get a raw HTML block that just includes","the `\u003cdel\u003e` tag (because it ends with the following blank","line).  So the contents get interpreted as CommonMark:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003cdel\u003e","","*foo*","","\u003c/del\u003e",".","\u003cdel\u003e","\u003cp\u003e\u003cem\u003efoo\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/del\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Finally, in these cases, the `\u003cdel\u003e` tags are interpreted","as [raw HTML] *inside* the CommonMark paragraph.  (Because","the tag is not on a line by itself, we get inline HTML","rather than an [HTML block].)","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003cdel\u003e*foo*\u003c/del\u003e",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cdel\u003e\u003cem\u003efoo\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/del\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003cdel","class=\"foo\"\u003e","*foo*","\u003c/del\u003e",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cdel","class=\"foo\"\u003e","\u003cem\u003efoo\u003c/em\u003e","\u003c/del\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","HTML tags designed to contain literal content","(`pre`, `script`, `style`, `textarea`), comments, processing instructions,","and declarations are treated somewhat differently.","Instead of ending at the first blank line, these blocks","end at the first line containing a corresponding end tag.","As a result, these blocks can contain blank lines:","","A pre tag (type 1):","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003cpre language=\"haskell\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003e","import Text.HTML.TagSoup","","main :: IO ()","main = print $ parseTags tags","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","okay",".","\u003cpre language=\"haskell\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003e","import Text.HTML.TagSoup","","main :: IO ()","main = print $ parseTags tags","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","\u003cp\u003eokay\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","A script tag (type 1):","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003cscript type=\"text/javascript\"\u003e","// JavaScript example","","document.getElementById(\"demo\").innerHTML = \"Hello JavaScript!\";","\u003c/script\u003e","okay",".","\u003cscript type=\"text/javascript\"\u003e","// JavaScript example","","document.getElementById(\"demo\").innerHTML = \"Hello JavaScript!\";","\u003c/script\u003e","\u003cp\u003eokay\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","A textarea tag (type 1):","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003ctextarea\u003e","","*foo*","","_bar_","","\u003c/textarea\u003e",".","\u003ctextarea\u003e","","*foo*","","_bar_","","\u003c/textarea\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","A style tag (type 1):","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003cstyle","  type=\"text/css\"\u003e","h1 {color:red;}","","p {color:blue;}","\u003c/style\u003e","okay",".","\u003cstyle","  type=\"text/css\"\u003e","h1 {color:red;}","","p {color:blue;}","\u003c/style\u003e","\u003cp\u003eokay\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","If there is no matching end tag, the block will end at the","end of the document (or the enclosing [block quote][block quotes]","or [list item][list items]):","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003cstyle","  type=\"text/css\"\u003e","","foo",".","\u003cstyle","  type=\"text/css\"\u003e","","foo","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003e \u003cdiv\u003e","\u003e foo","","bar",".","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003cdiv\u003e","foo","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","\u003cp\u003ebar\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","- \u003cdiv\u003e","- foo",".","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cdiv\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003cli\u003efoo\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","The end tag can occur on the same line as the start tag:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003cstyle\u003ep{color:red;}\u003c/style\u003e","*foo*",".","\u003cstyle\u003ep{color:red;}\u003c/style\u003e","\u003cp\u003e\u003cem\u003efoo\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003c!-- foo --\u003e*bar*","*baz*",".","\u003c!-- foo --\u003e*bar*","\u003cp\u003e\u003cem\u003ebaz\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Note that anything on the last line after the","end tag will be included in the [HTML block]:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003cscript\u003e","foo","\u003c/script\u003e1. *bar*",".","\u003cscript\u003e","foo","\u003c/script\u003e1. *bar*","````````````````````````````````","","","A comment (type 2):","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003c!-- Foo","","bar","   baz --\u003e","okay",".","\u003c!-- Foo","","bar","   baz --\u003e","\u003cp\u003eokay\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","","A processing instruction (type 3):","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003c?php","","  echo '\u003e';","","?\u003e","okay",".","\u003c?php","","  echo '\u003e';","","?\u003e","\u003cp\u003eokay\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","A declaration (type 4):","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003c!DOCTYPE html\u003e",".","\u003c!DOCTYPE html\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","CDATA (type 5):","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003c![CDATA[","function matchwo(a,b)","{","  if (a \u003c b \u0026\u0026 a \u003c 0) then {","    return 1;","","  } else {","","    return 0;","  }","}","]]\u003e","okay",".","\u003c![CDATA[","function matchwo(a,b)","{","  if (a \u003c b \u0026\u0026 a \u003c 0) then {","    return 1;","","  } else {","","    return 0;","  }","}","]]\u003e","\u003cp\u003eokay\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","The opening tag can be preceded by up to three spaces of indentation, but not","four:","","```````````````````````````````` example","  \u003c!-- foo --\u003e","","    \u003c!-- foo --\u003e",".","  \u003c!-- foo --\u003e","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u0026lt;!-- foo --\u0026gt;","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","  \u003cdiv\u003e","","    \u003cdiv\u003e",".","  \u003cdiv\u003e","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u0026lt;div\u0026gt;","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","An HTML block of types 1--6 can interrupt a paragraph, and need not be","preceded by a blank line.","","```````````````````````````````` example","Foo","\u003cdiv\u003e","bar","\u003c/div\u003e",".","\u003cp\u003eFoo\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cdiv\u003e","bar","\u003c/div\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","However, a following blank line is needed, except at the end of","a document, and except for blocks of types 1--5, [above][HTML","block]:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003cdiv\u003e","bar","\u003c/div\u003e","*foo*",".","\u003cdiv\u003e","bar","\u003c/div\u003e","*foo*","````````````````````````````````","","","HTML blocks of type 7 cannot interrupt a paragraph:","","```````````````````````````````` example","Foo","\u003ca href=\"bar\"\u003e","baz",".","\u003cp\u003eFoo","\u003ca href=\"bar\"\u003e","baz\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","This rule differs from John Gruber's original Markdown syntax","specification, which says:","","\u003e The only restrictions are that block-level HTML elements —","\u003e e.g. `\u003cdiv\u003e`, `\u003ctable\u003e`, `\u003cpre\u003e`, `\u003cp\u003e`, etc. — must be separated from","\u003e surrounding content by blank lines, and the start and end tags of the","\u003e block should not be indented with spaces or tabs.","","In some ways Gruber's rule is more restrictive than the one given","here:","","- It requires that an HTML block be preceded by a blank line.","- It does not allow the start tag to be indented.","- It requires a matching end tag, which it also does not allow to","  be indented.","","Most Markdown implementations (including some of Gruber's own) do not","respect all of these restrictions.","","There is one respect, however, in which Gruber's rule is more liberal","than the one given here, since it allows blank lines to occur inside","an HTML block.  There are two reasons for disallowing them here.","First, it removes the need to parse balanced tags, which is","expensive and can require backtracking from the end of the document","if no matching end tag is found. Second, it provides a very simple","and flexible way of including Markdown content inside HTML tags:","simply separate the Markdown from the HTML using blank lines:","","Compare:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003cdiv\u003e","","*Emphasized* text.","","\u003c/div\u003e",".","\u003cdiv\u003e","\u003cp\u003e\u003cem\u003eEmphasized\u003c/em\u003e text.\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/div\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003cdiv\u003e","*Emphasized* text.","\u003c/div\u003e",".","\u003cdiv\u003e","*Emphasized* text.","\u003c/div\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Some Markdown implementations have adopted a convention of","interpreting content inside tags as text if the open tag has","the attribute `markdown=1`.
