The rule given above seems a simpler and","more elegant way of achieving the same expressive power, which is also","much simpler to parse.","","The main potential drawback is that one can no longer paste HTML","blocks into Markdown documents with 100% reliability.  However,","*in most cases* this will work fine, because the blank lines in","HTML are usually followed by HTML block tags.  For example:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003ctable\u003e","","\u003ctr\u003e","","\u003ctd\u003e","Hi","\u003c/td\u003e","","\u003c/tr\u003e","","\u003c/table\u003e",".","\u003ctable\u003e","\u003ctr\u003e","\u003ctd\u003e","Hi","\u003c/td\u003e","\u003c/tr\u003e","\u003c/table\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","There are problems, however, if the inner tags are indented","*and* separated by spaces, as then they will be interpreted as","an indented code block:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003ctable\u003e","","  \u003ctr\u003e","","    \u003ctd\u003e","      Hi","    \u003c/td\u003e","","  \u003c/tr\u003e","","\u003c/table\u003e",".","\u003ctable\u003e","  \u003ctr\u003e","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u0026lt;td\u0026gt;","  Hi","\u0026lt;/td\u0026gt;","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","  \u003c/tr\u003e","\u003c/table\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Fortunately, blank lines are usually not necessary and can be","deleted.  The exception is inside `\u003cpre\u003e` tags, but as described","[above][HTML blocks], raw HTML blocks starting with `\u003cpre\u003e`","*can* contain blank lines.","","## Link reference definitions","","A [link reference definition](@)","consists of a [link label], optionally preceded by up to three spaces of","indentation, followed","by a colon (`:`), optional spaces or tabs (including up to one","[line ending]), a [link destination],","optional spaces or tabs (including up to one","[line ending]), and an optional [link","title], which if it is present must be separated","from the [link destination] by spaces or tabs.","No further character may occur.","","A [link reference definition]","does not correspond to a structural element of a document.  Instead, it","defines a label which can be used in [reference links]","and reference-style [images] elsewhere in the document.  [Link","reference definitions] can come either before or after the links that use","them.","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo]: /url \"title\"","","[foo]",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"/url\" title=\"title\"\u003efoo\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","   [foo]: ","      /url  ","           'the title'  ","","[foo]",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"/url\" title=\"the title\"\u003efoo\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","[Foo*bar\\]]:my_(url) 'title (with parens)'","","[Foo*bar\\]]",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"my_(url)\" title=\"title (with parens)\"\u003eFoo*bar]\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","[Foo bar]:","\u003cmy url\u003e","'title'","","[Foo bar]",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"my%20url\" title=\"title\"\u003eFoo bar\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","The title may extend over multiple lines:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo]: /url '","title","line1","line2","'","","[foo]",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"/url\" title=\"","title","line1","line2","\"\u003efoo\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","However, it may not contain a [blank line]:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo]: /url 'title","","with blank line'","","[foo]",".","\u003cp\u003e[foo]: /url 'title\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cp\u003ewith blank line'\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cp\u003e[foo]\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","The title may be omitted:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo]:","/url","","[foo]",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"/url\"\u003efoo\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","The link destination may not be omitted:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo]:","","[foo]",".","\u003cp\u003e[foo]:\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cp\u003e[foo]\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````",""," However, an empty link destination may be specified using"," angle brackets:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo]: \u003c\u003e","","[foo]",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"\"\u003efoo\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","The title must be separated from the link destination by","spaces or tabs:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo]: \u003cbar\u003e(baz)","","[foo]",".","\u003cp\u003e[foo]: \u003cbar\u003e(baz)\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cp\u003e[foo]\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Both title and destination can contain backslash escapes","and literal backslashes:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo]: /url\\bar\\*baz \"foo\\\"bar\\baz\"","","[foo]",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"/url%5Cbar*baz\" title=\"foo\u0026quot;bar\\baz\"\u003efoo\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","A link can come before its corresponding definition:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo]","","[foo]: url",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"url\"\u003efoo\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","If there are several matching definitions, the first one takes","precedence:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo]","","[foo]: first","[foo]: second",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"first\"\u003efoo\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","As noted in the section on [Links], matching of labels is","case-insensitive (see [matches]).","","```````````````````````````````` example","[FOO]: /url","","[Foo]",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"/url\"\u003eFoo\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","[ΑΓΩ]: /φου","","[αγω]",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"/%CF%86%CE%BF%CF%85\"\u003eαγω\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Whether something is a [link reference definition] is","independent of whether the link reference it defines is","used in the document.  Thus, for example, the following","document contains just a link reference definition, and","no visible content:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo]: /url",".","````````````````````````````````","","","Here is another one:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[","foo","]: /url","bar",".","\u003cp\u003ebar\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","This is not a link reference definition, because there are","characters other than spaces or tabs after the title:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo]: /url \"title\" ok",".","\u003cp\u003e[foo]: /url \u0026quot;title\u0026quot; ok\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","This is a link reference definition, but it has no title:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo]: /url","\"title\" ok",".","\u003cp\u003e\u0026quot;title\u0026quot; ok\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","This is not a link reference definition, because it is indented","four spaces:","","```````````````````````````````` example","    [foo]: /url \"title\"","","[foo]",".","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003e[foo]: /url \u0026quot;title\u0026quot;","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","\u003cp\u003e[foo]\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","This is not a link reference definition, because it occurs inside","a code block:","","```````````````````````````````` example","```","[foo]: /url","```","","[foo]",".","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003e[foo]: /url","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","\u003cp\u003e[foo]\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","A [link reference definition] cannot interrupt a paragraph.","","```````````````````````````````` example","Foo","[bar]: /baz","","[bar]",".","\u003cp\u003eFoo","[bar]: /baz\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cp\u003e[bar]\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","However, it can directly follow other block elements, such as headings","and thematic breaks, and it need not be followed by a blank line.","","```````````````````````````````` example","# [Foo]","[foo]: /url","\u003e bar",".","\u003ch1\u003e\u003ca href=\"/url\"\u003eFoo\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/h1\u003e","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003cp\u003ebar\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo]: /url","bar","===","[foo]",".","\u003ch1\u003ebar\u003c/h1\u003e","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"/url\"\u003efoo\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo]: /url","===","[foo]",".","\u003cp\u003e===","\u003ca href=\"/url\"\u003efoo\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Several [link reference definitions]","can occur one after another, without intervening blank lines.","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo]: /foo-url \"foo\"","[bar]: /bar-url","  \"bar\"","[baz]: /baz-url","","[foo],","[bar],","[baz]",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"/foo-url\" title=\"foo\"\u003efoo\u003c/a\u003e,","\u003ca href=\"/bar-url\" title=\"bar\"\u003ebar\u003c/a\u003e,","\u003ca href=\"/baz-url\"\u003ebaz\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","[Link reference definitions] can occur","inside block containers, like lists and block quotations.  They","affect the entire document, not just the container in which they","are defined:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo]","","\u003e [foo]: /url",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"/url\"\u003efoo\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","## Paragraphs","","A sequence of non-blank lines that cannot be interpreted as other","kinds of blocks forms a [paragraph](@).","The contents of the paragraph are the result of parsing the","paragraph's raw content as inlines.  The paragraph's raw content","is formed by concatenating the lines and removing initial and final","spaces or tabs.","","A simple example with two paragraphs:","","```````````````````````````````` example","aaa","","bbb",".","\u003cp\u003eaaa\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cp\u003ebbb\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Paragraphs can contain multiple lines, but no blank lines:","","```````````````````````````````` example","aaa","bbb","","ccc","ddd",".","\u003cp\u003eaaa","bbb\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cp\u003eccc","ddd\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Multiple blank lines between paragraphs have no effect:","","```````````````````````````````` example","aaa","","","bbb",".","\u003cp\u003eaaa\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cp\u003ebbb\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Leading spaces or tabs are skipped:","","```````````````````````````````` example","  aaa"," bbb",".","\u003cp\u003eaaa","bbb\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Lines after the first may be indented any amount, since indented","code blocks cannot interrupt paragraphs.","","```````````````````````````````` example","aaa","             bbb","                                       ccc",".","\u003cp\u003eaaa","bbb","ccc\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","However, the first line may be preceded by up to three spaces of indentation.","Four spaces of indentation is too many:","","```````````````````````````````` example","   aaa","bbb",".","\u003cp\u003eaaa","bbb\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","    aaa","bbb",".","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003eaaa","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","\u003cp\u003ebbb\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Final spaces or tabs are stripped before inline parsing, so a paragraph","that ends with two or more spaces will not end with a [hard line","break]:","","```````````````````````````````` example","aaa     ","bbb     ",".","\u003cp\u003eaaa\u003cbr /\u003e","bbb\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","## Blank lines","","[Blank lines] between block-level elements are ignored,","except for the role they play in determining whether a [list]","is [tight] or [loose].","","Blank lines at the beginning and end of the document are also ignored.","","```````````````````````````````` example","  ","","aaa","  ","","# aaa","","  ",".","\u003cp\u003eaaa\u003c/p\u003e","\u003ch1\u003eaaa\u003c/h1\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","","# Container blocks","","A [container block](#container-blocks) is a block that has other","blocks as its contents.  There are two basic kinds of container blocks:","[block quotes] and [list items].","[Lists] are meta-containers for [list items].","","We define the syntax for container blocks recursively.  The general","form of the definition is:","","\u003e If X is a sequence of blocks, then the result of","\u003e transforming X in such-and-such a way is a container of type Y","\u003e with these blocks as its content.","","So, we explain what counts as a block quote or list item by explaining","how these can be *generated* from their contents. This should suffice","to define the syntax, although it does not give a recipe for *parsing*","these constructions.  (A recipe is provided below in the section entitled","[A parsing strategy](#appendix-a-parsing-strategy).)","","## Block quotes","","A [block quote marker](@),","optionally preceded by up to three spaces of indentation,","consists of (a) the character `\u003e` together with a following space of","indentation, or (b) a single character `\u003e` not followed by a space of","indentation.","","The following rules define [block quotes]:","","1.  **Basic case.**  If a string of lines *Ls* constitute a sequence","    of blocks *Bs*, then the result of prepending a [block quote","    marker] to the beginning of each line in *Ls*","    is a [block quote](#block-quotes) containing *Bs*.","","2.  **Laziness.**  If a string of lines *Ls* constitute a [block","    quote](#block-quotes) with contents *Bs*, then the result of deleting","    the initial [block quote marker] from one or","    more lines in which the next character other than a space or tab after the","    [block quote marker] is [paragraph continuation","    text] is a block quote with *Bs* as its content.","    [Paragraph continuation text](@) is text","    that will be parsed as part of the content of a paragraph, but does","    not occur at the beginning of the paragraph.","","3.  **Consecutiveness.**  A document cannot contain two [block","    quotes] in a row unless there is a [blank line] between them.","","Nothing else counts as a [block quote](#block-quotes).","","Here is a simple example:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003e # Foo","\u003e bar","\u003e baz",".","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003ch1\u003eFoo\u003c/h1\u003e","\u003cp\u003ebar","baz\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","The space or tab after the `\u003e` characters can be omitted:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003e# Foo","\u003ebar","\u003e baz",".","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003ch1\u003eFoo\u003c/h1\u003e","\u003cp\u003ebar","baz\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","The `\u003e` characters can be preceded by up to three spaces of indentation:","","```````````````````````````````` example","   \u003e # Foo","   \u003e bar"," \u003e baz",".","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003ch1\u003eFoo\u003c/h1\u003e","\u003cp\u003ebar","baz\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Four spaces of indentation is too many:","","```````````````````````````````` example","    \u003e # Foo","    \u003e bar","    \u003e baz",".","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u0026gt; # Foo","\u0026gt; bar","\u0026gt; baz","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","The Laziness clause allows us to omit the `\u003e` before","[paragraph continuation text]:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003e # Foo","\u003e bar","baz",".","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003ch1\u003eFoo\u003c/h1\u003e","\u003cp\u003ebar","baz\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","A block quote can contain some lazy and some non-lazy","continuation lines:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003e bar","baz","\u003e foo",".","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003cp\u003ebar","baz","foo\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Laziness only applies to lines that would have been continuations of","paragraphs had they been prepended with [block quote markers].","For example, the `\u003e ` cannot be omitted in the second line of","","``` markdown","\u003e foo","\u003e ---","```","","without changing the meaning:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003e foo","---",".","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003cp\u003efoo\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","\u003chr /\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Similarly, if we omit the `\u003e ` in the second line of","","``` markdown","\u003e - foo","\u003e - bar","```","","then the block quote ends after the first line:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003e - foo","- bar",".","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003efoo\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003ebar\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","For the same reason, we can't omit the `\u003e ` in front of","subsequent lines of an indented or fenced code block:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003e     foo","    bar",".","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003efoo","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003ebar","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003e ```","foo","```",".","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","\u003cp\u003efoo\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Note that in the following case, we have a [lazy","continuation line]:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003e foo","    - bar",".","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003cp\u003efoo","- bar\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","To see why, note that in","","```markdown","\u003e foo","\u003e     - bar","```","","the `- bar` is indented too far to start a list, and can't","be an indented code block because indented code blocks cannot","interrupt paragraphs, so it is [paragraph continuation text].","","A block quote can be empty:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003e",".","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003e","\u003e  ","\u003e ",".","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","A block quote can have initial or final blank lines:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003e","\u003e foo","\u003e  ",".","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003cp\u003efoo\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","A blank line always separates block quotes:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003e foo","","\u003e bar",".","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003cp\u003efoo\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003cp\u003ebar\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","(Most current Markdown implementations, including John Gruber's","original `Markdown.pl`, will parse this example as a single block quote","with two paragraphs.  But it seems better to allow the author to decide","whether two block quotes or one are wanted.)","","Consecutiveness means that if we put these block quotes together,","we get a single block quote:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003e foo","\u003e bar",".","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003cp\u003efoo","bar\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","To get a block quote with two paragraphs, use:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003e foo","\u003e","\u003e bar",".","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003cp\u003efoo\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cp\u003ebar\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Block quotes can interrupt paragraphs:","","```````````````````````````````` example","foo","\u003e bar",".","\u003cp\u003efoo\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003cp\u003ebar\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","In general, blank lines are not needed before or after block","quotes:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003e aaa","***","\u003e bbb",".","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003cp\u003eaaa\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","\u003chr /\u003e","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003cp\u003ebbb\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","However, because of laziness, a blank line is needed between","a block quote and a following paragraph:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003e bar","baz",".","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003cp\u003ebar","baz\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003e bar","","baz",".","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003cp\u003ebar\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","\u003cp\u003ebaz\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003e bar","\u003e","baz",".","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003cp\u003ebar\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","\u003cp\u003ebaz\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","It is a consequence of the Laziness rule that any number","of initial `\u003e`s may be omitted on a continuation line of a","nested block quote:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003e \u003e \u003e foo","bar",".","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003cp\u003efoo","bar\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003e\u003e\u003e foo","\u003e bar","\u003e\u003ebaz",".","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003cp\u003efoo","bar","baz\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","When including an indented code block in a block quote,","remember that the [block quote marker] includes","both the `\u003e` and a following space of indentation.  So *five spaces* are needed","after the `\u003e`:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003e     code","","\u003e    not code",".","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003ecode","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003cp\u003enot code\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","","## List items","","A [list marker](@) is a","[bullet list marker] or an [ordered list marker].","","A [bullet list marker](@)","is a `-`, `+`, or `*` character.","","An [ordered list marker](@)","is a sequence of 1--9 arabic digits (`0-9`), followed by either a","`.` character or a `)` character.  (The reason for the length","limit is that with 10 digits we start seeing integer overflows","in some browsers.)","","The following rules define [list items]:","","1.  **Basic case.**  If a sequence of lines *Ls* constitute a sequence of","    blocks *Bs* starting with a character other than a space or tab, and *M* is","    a list marker of width *W* followed by 1 ≤ *N* ≤ 4 spaces of indentation,","    then the result of prepending *M* and the following spaces to the first line","    of *Ls*, and indenting subsequent lines of *Ls* by *W + N* spaces, is a","    list item with *Bs* as its contents.  The type of the list item","    (bullet or ordered) is determined by the type of its list marker.","    If the list item is ordered, then it is also assigned a start","    number, based on the ordered list marker.","","    Exceptions:","","    1. When the first list item in a [list] interrupts","       a paragraph---that is, when it starts on a line that would","       otherwise count as [paragraph continuation text]---then (a)","       the lines *Ls* must not begin with a blank line, and (b) if","       the list item is ordered, the start number must be 1.","    2. If any line is a [thematic break][thematic breaks] then","       that line is not a list item.","","For example, let *Ls* be the lines","","```````````````````````````````` example","A paragraph","with two lines.","","    indented code","","\u003e A block quote.",".","\u003cp\u003eA paragraph","with two lines.\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003eindented code","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003cp\u003eA block quote.\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","And let *M* be the marker `1.`, and *N* = 2.  Then rule #1 says","that the following is an ordered list item with start number 1,","and the same contents as *Ls*:","","```````````````````````````````` example","1.  A paragraph","    with two lines.","","        indented code","","    \u003e A block quote.",".","\u003col\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cp\u003eA paragraph","with two lines.\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003eindented code","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003cp\u003eA block quote.\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ol\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","The most important thing to notice is that the position of","the text after the list marker determines how much indentation","is needed in subsequent blocks in the list item.  If the list","marker takes up two spaces of indentation, and there are three spaces between","the list marker and the next character other than a space or tab, then blocks","must be indented five spaces in order to fall under the list","item.","","Here are some examples showing how far content must be indented to be","put under the list item:","","```````````````````````````````` example","- one",""," two",".","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003eone\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","\u003cp\u003etwo\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","- one","","  two",".","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cp\u003eone\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cp\u003etwo\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example"," -    one","","     two",".","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003eone\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003e two","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example"," -    one","","      two",".","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cp\u003eone\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cp\u003etwo\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","It is tempting to think of this in terms of columns:  the continuation","blocks must be indented at least to the column of the first character other than","a space or tab after the list marker.  However, that is not quite right.","The spaces of indentation after the list marker determine how much relative","indentation is needed.  Which column this indentation reaches will depend on","how the list item is embedded in other constructions, as shown by","this example:","","```````````````````````````````` example","   \u003e \u003e 1.  one","\u003e\u003e","\u003e\u003e     two",".","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003col\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cp\u003eone\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cp\u003etwo\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ol\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Here `two` occurs in the same column as the list marker `1.`,","but is actually contained in the list item, because there is","sufficient indentation after the last containing blockquote marker.","","The converse is also possible.  In the following example, the word `two`","occurs far to the right of the initial text of the list item, `one`, but","it is not considered part of the list item, because it is not indented","far enough past the blockquote marker:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003e\u003e- one","\u003e\u003e","  \u003e  \u003e two",".","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003eone\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","\u003cp\u003etwo\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Note that at least one space or tab is needed between the list marker and","any following content, so these are not list items:","","```````````````````````````````` example","-one","","2.two",".","\u003cp\u003e-one\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cp\u003e2.two\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","A list item may contain blocks that are separated by more than","one blank line.","","```````````````````````````````` example","- foo","","","  bar",".","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cp\u003efoo\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cp\u003ebar\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","A list item may contain any kind of block:","","```````````````````````````````` example","1.  foo","","    ```","    bar","    ```","","    baz","","    \u003e bam",".","\u003col\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cp\u003efoo\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003ebar","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","\u003cp\u003ebaz\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003cp\u003ebam\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ol\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","A list item that contains an indented code block will preserve","empty lines within the code block verbatim.","","```````````````````````````````` example","- Foo","","      bar","","","      baz",".","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cp\u003eFoo\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003ebar","","","baz","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","Note that ordered list start numbers must be nine digits or less:","","```````````````````````````````` example","123456789. ok",".","\u003col start=\"123456789\"\u003e","\u003cli\u003eok\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ol\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","1234567890. not ok",".","\u003cp\u003e1234567890. not ok\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","A start number may begin with 0s:","","```````````````````````````````` example","0. ok",".","\u003col start=\"0\"\u003e","\u003cli\u003eok\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ol\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","003. ok",".","\u003col start=\"3\"\u003e","\u003cli\u003eok\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ol\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","A start number may not be negative:","","```````````````````````````````` example","-1. not ok",".","\u003cp\u003e-1. not ok\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","","2.  **Item starting with indented code.**  If a sequence of lines *Ls*","    constitute a sequence of blocks *Bs* starting with an indented code","    block, and *M* is a list marker of width *W* followed by","    one space of indentation, then the result of prepending *M* and the","    following space to the first line of *Ls*, and indenting subsequent lines","    of *Ls* by *W + 1* spaces, is a list item with *Bs* as its contents.","    If a line is empty, then it need not be indented.  The type of the","    list item (bullet or ordered) is determined by the type of its list","    marker.  If the list item is ordered, then it is also assigned a","    start number, based on the ordered list marker.","","An indented code block will have to be preceded by four spaces of indentation","beyond the edge of the region where text will be included in the list item.","In the following case that is 6 spaces:","","```````````````````````````````` example","- foo","","      bar",".","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cp\u003efoo\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003ebar","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","And in this case it is 11 spaces:","","```````````````````````````````` example","  10.  foo","","           bar",".","\u003col start=\"10\"\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cp\u003efoo\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003ebar","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ol\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","If the *first* block in the list item is an indented code block,","then by rule #2, the contents must be preceded by *one* space of indentation","after the list marker:","","```````````````````````````````` example","    indented code","","paragraph","","    more code",".","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003eindented code","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","\u003cp\u003eparagraph\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003emore code","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","1.     indented code","","   paragraph","","       more code",".","\u003col\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003eindented code","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","\u003cp\u003eparagraph\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003emore code","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ol\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Note that an additional space of indentation is interpreted as space","inside the code block:","","```````````````````````````````` example","1.      indented code","","   paragraph","","       more code",".","\u003col\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003e indented code","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","\u003cp\u003eparagraph\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003emore code","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ol\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Note that rules #1 and #2 only apply to two cases:  (a) cases","in which the lines to be included in a list item begin with a","character other than a space or tab, and (b) cases in which","they begin with an indented code","block.  In a case like the following, where the first block begins with","three spaces of indentation, the rules do not allow us to form a list item by","indenting the whole thing and prepending a list marker:","","```````````````````````````````` example","   foo","","bar",".","\u003cp\u003efoo\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cp\u003ebar\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","-    foo","","  bar",".","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003efoo\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","\u003cp\u003ebar\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","This is not a significant restriction, because when a block is preceded by up to","three spaces of indentation, the indentation can always be removed without","a change in interpretation, allowing rule #1 to be applied.  So, in","the above case:","","```````````````````````````````` example","-  foo","","   bar",".","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cp\u003efoo\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cp\u003ebar\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","3.  **Item starting with a blank line.**  If a sequence of lines *Ls*","    starting with a single [blank line] constitute a (possibly empty)","    sequence of blocks *Bs*, and *M* is a list marker of width *W*,","    then the result of prepending *M* to the first line of *Ls*, and","    preceding subsequent lines of *Ls* by *W + 1* spaces of indentation, is a","    list item with *Bs* as its contents.","    If a line is empty, then it need not be indented.  The type of the","    list item (bullet or ordered) is determined by the type of its list","    marker.  If the list item is ordered, then it is also assigned a","    start number, based on the ordered list marker.","","Here are some list items that start with a blank line but are not empty:","","```````````````````````````````` example","-","  foo","-","  ```","  bar","  ```","-","      baz",".","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003efoo\u003c/li\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003ebar","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003ebaz","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","When the list item starts with a blank line, the number of spaces","following the list marker doesn't change the required indentation:","","```````````````````````````````` example","-   ","  foo",".","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003efoo\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","A list item can begin with at most one blank line.","In the following example, `foo` is not part of the list","item:","","```````````````````````````````` example","-","","  foo",".","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003e\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","\u003cp\u003efoo\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Here is an empty bullet list item:","","```````````````````````````````` example","- foo","-","- bar",".","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003efoo\u003c/li\u003e","\u003cli\u003e\u003c/li\u003e","\u003cli\u003ebar\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","It does not matter whether there are spaces or tabs following the [list marker]:","","```````````````````````````````` example","- foo","-   ","- bar",".","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003efoo\u003c/li\u003e","\u003cli\u003e\u003c/li\u003e","\u003cli\u003ebar\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Here is an empty ordered list item:","","```````````````````````````````` example","1. foo","2.","3. bar",".","\u003col\u003e","\u003cli\u003efoo\u003c/li\u003e","\u003cli\u003e\u003c/li\u003e","\u003cli\u003ebar\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ol\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","A list may start or end with an empty list item:","","```````````````````````````````` example","*",".","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003e\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","However, an empty list item cannot interrupt a paragraph:","","```````````````````````````````` example","foo","*","","foo","1.",".","\u003cp\u003efoo","*\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cp\u003efoo","1.\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","4.  **Indentation.**  If a sequence of lines *Ls* constitutes a list item","    according to rule #1, #2, or #3, then the result of preceding each line","    of *Ls* by up to three spaces of indentation (the same for each line) also","    constitutes a list item with the same contents and attributes.  If a line is","    empty, then it need not be indented.","","Indented one space:","","```````````````````````````````` example"," 1.  A paragraph","     with two lines.","","         indented code","","     \u003e A block quote.",".","\u003col\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cp\u003eA paragraph","with two lines.\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003eindented code","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003cp\u003eA block quote.\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ol\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Indented two spaces:","","```````````````````````````````` example","  1.  A paragraph","      with two lines.","","          indented code","","      \u003e A block quote.",".","\u003col\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cp\u003eA paragraph","with two lines.\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003eindented code","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003cp\u003eA block quote.\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ol\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Indented three spaces:","","```````````````````````````````` example","   1.  A paragraph","       with two lines.","","           indented code","","       \u003e A block quote.",".","\u003col\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cp\u003eA paragraph","with two lines.\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003eindented code","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003cp\u003eA block quote.\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ol\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Four spaces indent gives a code block:","","```````````````````````````````` example","    1.  A paragraph","        with two lines.","","            indented code","","        \u003e A block quote.",".","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003e1.  A paragraph","    with two lines.","","        indented code","","    \u0026gt; A block quote.","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","","5.  **Laziness.**  If a string of lines *Ls* constitute a [list","    item](#list-items) with contents *Bs*, then the result of deleting","    some or all of the indentation from one or more lines in which the","    next character other than a space or tab after the indentation is","    [paragraph continuation text] is a","    list item with the same contents and attributes.  The unindented","    lines are called","    [lazy continuation line](@)s.","","Here is an example with [lazy continuation lines]:","","```````````````````````````````` example","  1.  A paragraph","with two lines.","","          indented code","","      \u003e A block quote.",".","\u003col\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cp\u003eA paragraph","with two lines.\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003eindented code","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003cp\u003eA block quote.\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ol\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Indentation can be partially deleted:","","```````````````````````````````` example","  1.  A paragraph","    with two lines.",".","\u003col\u003e","\u003cli\u003eA paragraph","with two lines.\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ol\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","These examples show how laziness can work in nested structures:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003e 1. \u003e Blockquote","continued here.",".","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003col\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003cp\u003eBlockquote","continued here.\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ol\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003e 1. \u003e Blockquote","\u003e continued here.",".","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003col\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003cp\u003eBlockquote","continued here.\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ol\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","","6.  **That's all.** Nothing that is not counted as a list item by rules","    #1--5 counts as a [list item](#list-items).","","The rules for sublists follow from the general rules","[above][List items].  A sublist must be indented the same number","of spaces of indentation a paragraph would need to be in order to be included","in the list item.","","So, in this case we need two spaces indent:","","```````````````````````````````` example","- foo","  - bar","    - baz","      - boo",".","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003efoo","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003ebar","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003ebaz","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003eboo\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","One is not enough:","","```````````````````````````````` example","- foo"," - bar","  - baz","   - boo",".","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003efoo\u003c/li\u003e","\u003cli\u003ebar\u003c/li\u003e","\u003cli\u003ebaz\u003c/li\u003e","\u003cli\u003eboo\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Here we need four, because the list marker is wider:","","```````````````````````````````` example","10) foo","    - bar",".","\u003col start=\"10\"\u003e","\u003cli\u003efoo","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003ebar\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ol\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Three is not enough:","","```````````````````````````````` example","10) foo","   - bar",".","\u003col start=\"10\"\u003e","\u003cli\u003efoo\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ol\u003e","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003ebar\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","A list may be the first block in a list item:","","```````````````````````````````` example","- - foo",".","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003efoo\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","1. - 2. foo",".","\u003col\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003col start=\"2\"\u003e","\u003cli\u003efoo\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ol\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ol\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","A list item can contain a heading:","","```````````````````````````````` example","- # Foo","- Bar","  ---","  baz",".","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003ch1\u003eFoo\u003c/h1\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003ch2\u003eBar\u003c/h2\u003e","baz\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","### Motivation","","John Gruber's Markdown spec says the following about list items:","","1. \"List markers typically start at the left margin, but may be indented","   by up to three spaces. List markers must be followed by one or more","   spaces or a tab.\"","","2. \"To make lists look nice, you can wrap items with hanging indents....","   But if you don't want to, you don't have to.\"","","3. \"List items may consist of multiple paragraphs. Each subsequent","   paragraph in a list item must be indented by either 4 spaces or one","   tab.\"","","4. \"It looks nice if you indent every line of the subsequent paragraphs,","   but here again, Markdown will allow you to be lazy.\"","","5. \"To put a blockquote within a list item, the blockquote's `\u003e`","   delimiters need to be indented.\"","","6. \"To put a code block within a list item, the code block needs to be","   indented twice — 8 spaces or two tabs.\"","","These rules specify that a paragraph under a list item must be indented","four spaces (presumably, from the left margin, rather than the start of","the list marker, but this is not said), and that code under a list item","must be indented eight spaces instead of the usual four.  They also say","that a block quote must be indented, but not by how much; however, the","example given has four spaces indentation.  Although nothing is said","about other kinds of block-level content, it is certainly reasonable to","infer that *all* block elements under a list item, including other","lists, must be indented four spaces.  This principle has been called the","*four-space rule*.","","The four-space rule is clear and principled, and if the reference","implementation `Markdown.pl` had followed it, it probably would have","become the standard.  However, `Markdown.pl` allowed paragraphs and","sublists to start with only two spaces indentation, at least on the","outer level.  Worse, its behavior was inconsistent: a sublist of an","outer-level list needed two spaces indentation, but a sublist of this","sublist needed three spaces.  It is not surprising, then, that different","implementations of Markdown have developed very different rules for","determining what comes under a list item.  (Pandoc and python-Markdown,","for example, stuck with Gruber's syntax description and the four-space","rule, while discount, redcarpet, marked, PHP Markdown, and others","followed `Markdown.pl`'s behavior more closely.)","","Unfortunately, given the divergences between implementations, there","is no way to give a spec for list items that will be guaranteed not","to break any existing documents.  However, the spec given here should","correctly handle lists formatted with either the four-space rule or","the more forgiving `Markdown.pl` behavior, provided they are laid out","in a way that is natural for a human to read.","","The strategy here is to let the width and indentation of the list marker","determine the indentation necessary for blocks to fall under the list","item, rather than having a fixed and arbitrary number.  The writer can","think of the body of the list item as a unit which gets indented to the","right enough to fit the list marker (and any indentation on the list","marker).  (The laziness rule, #5, then allows continuation lines to be","unindented if needed.)","","This rule is superior, we claim, to any rule requiring a fixed level of","indentation from the margin.  The four-space rule is clear but","unnatural. It is quite unintuitive that","","``` markdown","- foo","","  bar","","  - baz","```","","should be parsed as two lists with an intervening paragraph,","","``` html","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003efoo\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","\u003cp\u003ebar\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003ebaz\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","```","","as the four-space rule demands, rather than a single list,","","``` html","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cp\u003efoo\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cp\u003ebar\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003ebaz\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","```","","The choice of four spaces is arbitrary.  It can be learned, but it is","not likely to be guessed, and it trips up beginners regularly.","","Would it help to adopt a two-space rule?  The problem is that such","a rule, together with the rule allowing up to three spaces of indentation for","the initial list marker, allows text that is indented *less than* the","original list marker to be included in the list item. For example,","`Markdown.pl` parses","","``` markdown","   - one","","  two","```","","as a single list item, with `two` a continuation paragraph:","","``` html","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cp\u003eone\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cp\u003etwo\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","```","","and similarly","","``` markdown","\u003e   - one","\u003e","\u003e  two","```","","as","","``` html","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cp\u003eone\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cp\u003etwo\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","```","","This is extremely unintuitive.","","Rather than requiring a fixed indent from the margin, we could require","a fixed indent (say, two spaces, or even one space) from the list marker (which","may itself be indented).  This proposal would remove the last anomaly","discussed.  Unlike the spec presented above, it would count the following","as a list item with a subparagraph, even though the paragraph `bar`","is not indented as far as the first paragraph `foo`:","","``` markdown"," 10. foo","","   bar  ","```","","Arguably this text does read like a list item with `bar` as a subparagraph,","which may count in favor of the proposal.  However, on this proposal indented","code would have to be indented six spaces after the list marker.  And this","would break a lot of existing Markdown, which has the pattern:","","``` markdown","1.  foo","","        indented code","```","","where the code is indented eight spaces.  The spec above, by contrast, will","parse this text as expected, since the code block's indentation is measured","from the beginning of `foo`.","","The one case that needs special treatment is a list item that *starts*","with indented code.  How much indentation is required in that case, since","we don't have a \"first paragraph\" to measure from?  Rule #2 simply stipulates","that in such cases, we require one space indentation from the list marker","(and then the normal four spaces for the indented code).  This will match the","four-space rule in cases where the list marker plus its initial indentation","takes four spaces (a common case), but diverge in other cases.","","## Lists","","A [list](@) is a sequence of one or more","list items [of the same type].  The list items","may be separated by any number of blank lines.","","Two list items are [of the same type](@)","if they begin with a [list marker] of the same type.","Two list markers are of the","same type if (a) they are bullet list markers using the same character","(`-`, `+`, or `*`) or (b) they are ordered list numbers with the same","delimiter (either `.` or `)`).","","A list is an [ordered list](@)","if its constituent list items begin with","[ordered list markers], and a","[bullet list](@) if its constituent list","items begin with [bullet list markers].","","The [start number](@)","of an [ordered list] is determined by the list number of","its initial list item.  The numbers of subsequent list items are","disregarded.","","A list is [loose](@) if any of its constituent","list items are separated by blank lines, or if any of its constituent","list items directly contain two block-level elements with a blank line","between them.  Otherwise a list is [tight](@).","(The difference in HTML output is that paragraphs in a loose list are","wrapped in `\u003cp\u003e` tags, while paragraphs in a tight list are not.)","","Changing the bullet or ordered list delimiter starts a new list:","","```````````````````````````````` example","- foo","- bar","+ baz",".","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003efoo\u003c/li\u003e","\u003cli\u003ebar\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003ebaz\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","1. foo","2. bar","3) baz",".","\u003col\u003e","\u003cli\u003efoo\u003c/li\u003e","\u003cli\u003ebar\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ol\u003e","\u003col start=\"3\"\u003e","\u003cli\u003ebaz\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ol\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","In CommonMark, a list can interrupt a paragraph. That is,","no blank line is needed to separate a paragraph from a following","list:","","```````````````````````````````` example","Foo","- bar","- baz",".","\u003cp\u003eFoo\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003ebar\u003c/li\u003e","\u003cli\u003ebaz\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","`Markdown.pl` does not allow this, through fear of triggering a list","via a numeral in a hard-wrapped line:","","``` markdown","The number of windows in my house is","14.  The number of doors is 6.","```","","Oddly, though, `Markdown.pl` *does* allow a blockquote to","interrupt a paragraph, even though the same considerations might","apply.","","In CommonMark, we do allow lists to interrupt paragraphs, for","two reasons.  First, it is natural and not uncommon for people","to start lists without blank lines:","","``` markdown","I need to buy","- new shoes","- a coat","- a plane ticket","```","","Second, we are attracted to a","","\u003e [principle of uniformity](@):","\u003e if a chunk of text has a certain","\u003e meaning, it will continue to have the same meaning when put into a","\u003e container block (such as a list item or blockquote).","","(Indeed, the spec for [list items] and [block quotes] presupposes","this principle.) This principle implies that if","","``` markdown","  * I need to buy","    - new shoes","    - a coat","    - a plane ticket","```","","is a list item containing a paragraph followed by a nested sublist,","as all Markdown implementations agree it is (though the paragraph","may be rendered without `\u003cp\u003e` tags, since the list is \"tight\"),","then","","``` markdown","I need to buy","- new shoes","- a coat","- a plane ticket","```","","by itself should be a paragraph followed by a nested sublist.","","Since it is well established Markdown practice to allow lists to","interrupt paragraphs inside list items, the [principle of","uniformity] requires us to allow this outside list items as","well.  ([reStructuredText](https://docutils.sourceforge.net/rst.html)","takes a different approach, requiring blank lines before lists","even inside other list items.)","","In order to solve the problem of unwanted lists in paragraphs with","hard-wrapped numerals, we allow only lists starting with `1` to","interrupt paragraphs.  Thus,","","```````````````````````````````` example","The number of windows in my house is","14.  The number of doors is 6.",".","\u003cp\u003eThe number of windows in my house is","14.  The number of doors is 6.\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","We may still get an unintended result in cases like","","```````````````````````````````` example","The number of windows in my house is","1.  The number of doors is 6.",".","\u003cp\u003eThe number of windows in my house is\u003c/p\u003e","\u003col\u003e","\u003cli\u003eThe number of doors is 6.\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ol\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","but this rule should prevent most spurious list captures.","","There can be any number of blank lines between items:","","```````````````````````````````` example","- foo","","- bar","","","- baz",".","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cp\u003efoo\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cp\u003ebar\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cp\u003ebaz\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","```````````````````````````````` example","- foo","  - bar","    - baz","","","      bim",".","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003efoo","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003ebar","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cp\u003ebaz\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cp\u003ebim\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","To separate consecutive lists of the same type, or to separate a","list from an indented code block that would otherwise be parsed","as a subparagraph of the final list item, you can insert a blank HTML","comment:","","```````````````````````````````` example","- foo","- bar","","\u003c!-- --\u003e","","- baz","- bim",".","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003efoo\u003c/li\u003e","\u003cli\u003ebar\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","\u003c!-- --\u003e","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003ebaz\u003c/li\u003e","\u003cli\u003ebim\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","-   foo","","    notcode","","-   foo","","\u003c!-- --\u003e","","    code",".","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cp\u003efoo\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cp\u003enotcode\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cp\u003efoo\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","\u003c!-- --\u003e","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003ecode","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","List items need not be indented to the same level.  The following","list items will be treated as items at the same list level,","since none is indented enough to belong to the previous list","item:","","```````````````````````````````` example","- a"," - b","  - c","   - d","  - e"," - f","- g",".","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003ea\u003c/li\u003e","\u003cli\u003eb\u003c/li\u003e","\u003cli\u003ec\u003c/li\u003e","\u003cli\u003ed\u003c/li\u003e","\u003cli\u003ee\u003c/li\u003e","\u003cli\u003ef\u003c/li\u003e","\u003cli\u003eg\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","1. a","","  2. b","","   3. c",".","\u003col\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cp\u003ea\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cp\u003eb\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cp\u003ec\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ol\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","Note, however, that list items may not be preceded by more than","three spaces of indentation.  Here `- e` is treated as a paragraph continuation","line, because it is indented more than three spaces:","","```````````````````````````````` example","- a"," - b","  - c","   - d","    - e",".","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003ea\u003c/li\u003e","\u003cli\u003eb\u003c/li\u003e","\u003cli\u003ec\u003c/li\u003e","\u003cli\u003ed","- e\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","And here, `3. c` is treated as in indented code block,","because it is indented four spaces and preceded by a","blank line.","","```````````````````````````````` example","1. a","","  2. b","","    3. c",".","\u003col\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cp\u003ea\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cp\u003eb\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ol\u003e","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003e3. c","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","This is a loose list, because there is a blank line between","two of the list items:","","```````````````````````````````` example","- a","- b","","- c",".","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cp\u003ea\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cp\u003eb\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cp\u003ec\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","So is this, with a empty second item:","","```````````````````````````````` example","* a","*","","* c",".","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cp\u003ea\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003cli\u003e\u003c/li\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cp\u003ec\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","These are loose lists, even though there are no blank lines between the items,","because one of the items directly contains two block-level elements","with a blank line between them:","","```````````````````````````````` example","- a","- b","","  c","- d",".","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cp\u003ea\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cp\u003eb\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cp\u003ec\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cp\u003ed\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","- a","- b","","  [ref]: /url","- d",".","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cp\u003ea\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cp\u003eb\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cp\u003ed\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","This is a tight list, because the blank lines are in a code block:","","```````````````````````````````` example","- a","- ```","  b","","","  ```","- c",".","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003ea\u003c/li\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003eb","","","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003cli\u003ec\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","This is a tight list, because the blank line is between two","paragraphs of a sublist.  So the sublist is loose while","the outer list is tight:","","```````````````````````````````` example","- a","  - b","","    c","- d",".","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003ea","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cp\u003eb\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cp\u003ec\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003cli\u003ed\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","This is a tight list, because the blank line is inside the","block quote:","","```````````````````````````````` example","* a","  \u003e b","  \u003e","* c",".","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003ea","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003cp\u003eb\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003cli\u003ec\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","This list is tight, because the consecutive block elements","are not separated by blank lines:","","```````````````````````````````` example","- a","  \u003e b","  ```","  c","  ```","- d",".","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003ea","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003cp\u003eb\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003ec","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003cli\u003ed\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","A single-paragraph list is tight:","","```````````````````````````````` example","- a",".","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003ea\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","- a","  - b",".","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003ea","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003eb\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","This list is loose, because of the blank line between the","two block elements in the list item:","","```````````````````````````````` example","1. ```","   foo","   ```","","   bar",".","\u003col\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003efoo","\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e","\u003cp\u003ebar\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ol\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Here the outer list is loose, the inner list tight:","","```````````````````````````````` example","* foo","  * bar","","  baz",".","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cp\u003efoo\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003ebar\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","\u003cp\u003ebaz\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","- a","  - b","  - c","","- d","  - e","  - f",".","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cp\u003ea\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003eb\u003c/li\u003e","\u003cli\u003ec\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003cli\u003e","\u003cp\u003ed\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cul\u003e","\u003cli\u003ee\u003c/li\u003e","\u003cli\u003ef\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","\u003c/li\u003e","\u003c/ul\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","# Inlines","","Inlines are parsed sequentially from the beginning of the character","stream to the end (left to right, in left-to-right languages).","Thus, for example, in","","```````````````````````````````` example","`hi`lo`",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ccode\u003ehi\u003c/code\u003elo`\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","`hi` is parsed as code, leaving the backtick at the end as a literal","backtick.","","","","## Code spans","","A [backtick string](@)","is a string of one or more backtick characters (`` ` ``) that is neither","preceded nor followed by a backtick.","","A [code span](@) begins with a backtick string and ends with","a backtick string of equal length.  The contents of the code span are","the characters between these two backtick strings, normalized in the","following ways:","","- First, [line endings] are converted to [spaces].","- If the resulting string both begins *and* ends with a [space]","  character, but does not consist entirely of [space]","  characters, a single [space] character is removed from the","  front and back.  This allows you to include code that begins","  or ends with backtick characters, which must be separated by","  whitespace from the opening or closing backtick strings.","","This is a simple code span:","","```````````````````````````````` example","`foo`",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ccode\u003efoo\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Here two backticks are used, because the code contains a backtick.","This example also illustrates stripping of a single leading and","trailing space:","","```````````````````````````````` example","`` foo ` bar ``",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ccode\u003efoo ` bar\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","This example shows the motivation for stripping leading and trailing","spaces:","","```````````````````````````````` example","` `` `",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ccode\u003e``\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","Note that only *one* space is stripped:","","```````````````````````````````` example","`  ``  `",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ccode\u003e `` \u003c/code\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","The stripping only happens if the space is on both","sides of the string:","","```````````````````````````````` example","` a`",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ccode\u003e a\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","Only [spaces], and not [unicode whitespace] in general, are","stripped in this way:","","```````````````````````````````` example","` b `",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ccode\u003e b \u003c/code\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","No stripping occurs if the code span contains only spaces:","","```````````````````````````````` example","` `","`  `",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ccode\u003e \u003c/code\u003e","\u003ccode\u003e  \u003c/code\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","[Line endings] are treated like spaces:","","```````````````````````````````` example","``","foo","bar  ","baz","``",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ccode\u003efoo bar   baz\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","```````````````````````````````` example","``","foo ","``",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ccode\u003efoo \u003c/code\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Interior spaces are not collapsed:","","```````````````````````````````` example","`foo   bar ","baz`",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ccode\u003efoo   bar  baz\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","Note that browsers will typically collapse consecutive spaces","when rendering `\u003ccode\u003e` elements, so it is recommended that","the following CSS be used:","","    code{white-space: pre-wrap;}","","","Note that backslash escapes do not work in code spans. All backslashes","are treated literally:","","```````````````````````````````` example","`foo\\`bar`",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ccode\u003efoo\\\u003c/code\u003ebar`\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Backslash escapes are never needed, because one can always choose a","string of *n* backtick characters as delimiters, where the code does","not contain any strings of exactly *n* backtick characters.","","```````````````````````````````` example","``foo`bar``",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ccode\u003efoo`bar\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","```````````````````````````````` example","` foo `` bar `",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ccode\u003efoo `` bar\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Code span backticks have higher precedence than any other inline","constructs except HTML tags and autolinks.  Thus, for example, this is","not parsed as emphasized text, since the second `*` is part of a code","span:","","```````````````````````````````` example","*foo`*`",".","\u003cp\u003e*foo\u003ccode\u003e*\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","And this is not parsed as a link:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[not a `link](/foo`)",".","\u003cp\u003e[not a \u003ccode\u003elink](/foo\u003c/code\u003e)\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Code spans, HTML tags, and autolinks have the same precedence.","Thus, this is code:","","```````````````````````````````` example","`\u003ca href=\"`\"\u003e`",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u0026lt;a href=\u0026quot;\u003c/code\u003e\u0026quot;\u0026gt;`\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","But this is an HTML tag:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003ca href=\"`\"\u003e`",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"`\"\u003e`\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","And this is code:","","```````````````````````````````` example","`\u003chttps://foo.bar.`baz\u003e`",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u0026lt;https://foo.bar.\u003c/code\u003ebaz\u0026gt;`\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","But this is an autolink:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003chttps://foo.bar.`baz\u003e`",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"https://foo.bar.%60baz\"\u003ehttps://foo.bar.`baz\u003c/a\u003e`\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","When a backtick string is not closed by a matching backtick string,","we just have literal backticks:","","```````````````````````````````` example","```foo``",".","\u003cp\u003e```foo``\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","`foo",".","\u003cp\u003e`foo\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","The following case also illustrates the need for opening and","closing backtick strings to be equal in length:","","```````````````````````````````` example","`foo``bar``",".","\u003cp\u003e`foo\u003ccode\u003ebar\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","## Emphasis and strong emphasis","","John Gruber's original [Markdown syntax","description](https://daringfireball.net/projects/markdown/syntax#em) says:","","\u003e Markdown treats asterisks (`*`) and underscores (`_`) as indicators of","\u003e emphasis. Text wrapped with one `*` or `_` will be wrapped with an HTML","\u003e `\u003cem\u003e` tag; double `*`'s or `_`'s will be wrapped with an HTML `\u003cstrong\u003e`","\u003e tag.","","This is enough for most users, but these rules leave much undecided,","especially when it comes to nested emphasis.  The original","`Markdown.pl` test suite makes it clear that triple `***` and","`___` delimiters can be used for strong emphasis, and most","implementations have also allowed the following patterns:","","``` markdown","***strong emph***","***strong** in emph*","***emph* in strong**","**in strong *emph***","*in emph **strong***","```","","The following patterns are less widely supported, but the intent","is clear and they are useful (especially in contexts like bibliography","entries):","","``` markdown","*emph *with emph* in it*","**strong **with strong** in it**","```","","Many implementations have also restricted intraword emphasis to","the `*` forms, to avoid unwanted emphasis in words containing","internal underscores.  (It is best practice to put these in code","spans, but users often do not.)","","``` markdown","internal emphasis: foo*bar*baz","no emphasis: foo_bar_baz","```","","The rules given below capture all of these patterns, while allowing","for efficient parsing strategies that do not backtrack.","","First, some definitions.  A [delimiter run](@) is either","a sequence of one or more `*` characters that is not preceded or","followed by a non-backslash-escaped `*` character, or a sequence","of one or more `_` characters that is not preceded or followed by","a non-backslash-escaped `_` character.","","A [left-flanking delimiter run](@) is","a [delimiter run] that is (1) not followed by [Unicode whitespace],","and either (2a) not followed by a [Unicode punctuation character], or","(2b) followed by a [Unicode punctuation character] and","preceded by [Unicode whitespace] or a [Unicode punctuation character].","For purposes of this definition, the beginning and the end of","the line count as Unicode whitespace.","","A [right-flanking delimiter run](@) is","a [delimiter run] that is (1) not preceded by [Unicode whitespace],","and either (2a) not preceded by a [Unicode punctuation character], or","(2b) preceded by a [Unicode punctuation character] and","followed by [Unicode whitespace] or a [Unicode punctuation character].","For purposes of this definition, the beginning and the end of","the line count as Unicode whitespace.","","Here are some examples of delimiter runs.","","  - left-flanking but not right-flanking:","","    ```","    ***abc","      _abc","    **\"abc\"","     _\"abc\"","    ```","","  - right-flanking but not left-flanking:","","    ```","     abc***","     abc_","    \"abc\"**","    \"abc\"_","    ```","","  - Both left and right-flanking:","","    ```","     abc***def","    \"abc\"_\"def\"","    ```","","  - Neither left nor right-flanking:","","    ```","    abc *** def","    a _ b","    ```","","(The idea of distinguishing left-flanking and right-flanking","delimiter runs based on the character before and the character","after comes from Roopesh Chander's","[vfmd](https://web.archive.org/web/20220608143320/http://www.vfmd.org/vfmd-spec/specification/#procedure-for-identifying-emphasis-tags).","vfmd uses the terminology \"emphasis indicator string\" instead of \"delimiter","run,\" and its rules for distinguishing left- and right-flanking runs","are a bit more complex than the ones given here.)","","The following rules define emphasis and strong emphasis:","","1.  A single `*` character [can open emphasis](@)","    iff (if and only if) it is part of a [left-flanking delimiter run].","","2.  A single `_` character [can open emphasis] iff","    it is part of a [left-flanking delimiter run]","    and either (a) not part of a [right-flanking delimiter run]","    or (b) part of a [right-flanking delimiter run]","    preceded by a [Unicode punctuation character].","","3.  A single `*` character [can close emphasis](@)","    iff it is part of a [right-flanking delimiter run].","","4.  A single `_` character [can close emphasis] iff","    it is part of a [right-flanking delimiter run]","    and either (a) not part of a [left-flanking delimiter run]","    or (b) part of a [left-flanking delimiter run]","    followed by a [Unicode punctuation character].","","5.  A double `**` [can open strong emphasis](@)","    iff it is part of a [left-flanking delimiter run].","","6.  A double `__` [can open strong emphasis] iff","    it is part of a [left-flanking delimiter run]","    and either (a) not part of a [right-flanking delimiter run]","    or (b) part of a [right-flanking delimiter run]","    preceded by a [Unicode punctuation character].","","7.  A double `**` [can close strong emphasis](@)","    iff it is part of a [right-flanking delimiter run].","","8.
