A double `__` [can close strong emphasis] iff","    it is part of a [right-flanking delimiter run]","    and either (a) not part of a [left-flanking delimiter run]","    or (b) part of a [left-flanking delimiter run]","    followed by a [Unicode punctuation character].","","9.  Emphasis begins with a delimiter that [can open emphasis] and ends","    with a delimiter that [can close emphasis], and that uses the same","    character (`_` or `*`) as the opening delimiter.  The","    opening and closing delimiters must belong to separate","    [delimiter runs].  If one of the delimiters can both","    open and close emphasis, then the sum of the lengths of the","    delimiter runs containing the opening and closing delimiters","    must not be a multiple of 3 unless both lengths are","    multiples of 3.","","10. Strong emphasis begins with a delimiter that","    [can open strong emphasis] and ends with a delimiter that","    [can close strong emphasis], and that uses the same character","    (`_` or `*`) as the opening delimiter.  The","    opening and closing delimiters must belong to separate","    [delimiter runs].  If one of the delimiters can both open","    and close strong emphasis, then the sum of the lengths of","    the delimiter runs containing the opening and closing","    delimiters must not be a multiple of 3 unless both lengths","    are multiples of 3.","","11. A literal `*` character cannot occur at the beginning or end of","    `*`-delimited emphasis or `**`-delimited strong emphasis, unless it","    is backslash-escaped.","","12. A literal `_` character cannot occur at the beginning or end of","    `_`-delimited emphasis or `__`-delimited strong emphasis, unless it","    is backslash-escaped.","","Where rules 1--12 above are compatible with multiple parsings,","the following principles resolve ambiguity:","","13. The number of nestings should be minimized. Thus, for example,","    an interpretation `\u003cstrong\u003e...\u003c/strong\u003e` is always preferred to","    `\u003cem\u003e\u003cem\u003e...\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/em\u003e`.","","14. An interpretation `\u003cem\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e...\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/em\u003e` is always","    preferred to `\u003cstrong\u003e\u003cem\u003e...\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e`.","","15. When two potential emphasis or strong emphasis spans overlap,","    so that the second begins before the first ends and ends after","    the first ends, the first takes precedence. Thus, for example,","    `*foo _bar* baz_` is parsed as `\u003cem\u003efoo _bar\u003c/em\u003e baz_` rather","    than `*foo \u003cem\u003ebar* baz\u003c/em\u003e`.","","16. When there are two potential emphasis or strong emphasis spans","    with the same closing delimiter, the shorter one (the one that","    opens later) takes precedence. Thus, for example,","    `**foo **bar baz**` is parsed as `**foo \u003cstrong\u003ebar baz\u003c/strong\u003e`","    rather than `\u003cstrong\u003efoo **bar baz\u003c/strong\u003e`.","","17. Inline code spans, links, images, and HTML tags group more tightly","    than emphasis.  So, when there is a choice between an interpretation","    that contains one of these elements and one that does not, the","    former always wins.  Thus, for example, `*[foo*](bar)` is","    parsed as `*\u003ca href=\"bar\"\u003efoo*\u003c/a\u003e` rather than as","    `\u003cem\u003e[foo\u003c/em\u003e](bar)`.","","These rules can be illustrated through a series of examples.","","Rule 1:","","```````````````````````````````` example","*foo bar*",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cem\u003efoo bar\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","This is not emphasis, because the opening `*` is followed by","whitespace, and hence not part of a [left-flanking delimiter run]:","","```````````````````````````````` example","a * foo bar*",".","\u003cp\u003ea * foo bar*\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","This is not emphasis, because the opening `*` is preceded","by an alphanumeric and followed by punctuation, and hence","not part of a [left-flanking delimiter run]:","","```````````````````````````````` example","a*\"foo\"*",".","\u003cp\u003ea*\u0026quot;foo\u0026quot;*\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Unicode nonbreaking spaces count as whitespace, too:","","```````````````````````````````` example","* a *",".","\u003cp\u003e* a *\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Unicode symbols count as punctuation, too:","","```````````````````````````````` example","*$*alpha.","","*£*bravo.","","*€*charlie.",".","\u003cp\u003e*$*alpha.\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cp\u003e*£*bravo.\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cp\u003e*€*charlie.\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Intraword emphasis with `*` is permitted:","","```````````````````````````````` example","foo*bar*",".","\u003cp\u003efoo\u003cem\u003ebar\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","5*6*78",".","\u003cp\u003e5\u003cem\u003e6\u003c/em\u003e78\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Rule 2:","","```````````````````````````````` example","_foo bar_",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cem\u003efoo bar\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","This is not emphasis, because the opening `_` is followed by","whitespace:","","```````````````````````````````` example","_ foo bar_",".","\u003cp\u003e_ foo bar_\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","This is not emphasis, because the opening `_` is preceded","by an alphanumeric and followed by punctuation:","","```````````````````````````````` example","a_\"foo\"_",".","\u003cp\u003ea_\u0026quot;foo\u0026quot;_\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Emphasis with `_` is not allowed inside words:","","```````````````````````````````` example","foo_bar_",".","\u003cp\u003efoo_bar_\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","пристаням_стремятся_",".","\u003cp\u003eпристаням_стремятся_\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Here `_` does not generate emphasis, because the first delimiter run","is right-flanking and the second left-flanking:","","```````````````````````````````` \u003cstrong\u003ebar\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","**foo *bar* baz**",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003efoo \u003cem\u003ebar\u003c/em\u003e baz\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","**foo*bar*baz**",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003efoo\u003cem\u003ebar\u003c/em\u003ebaz\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","***foo* bar**",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e\u003cem\u003efoo\u003c/em\u003e bar\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","**foo *bar***",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003efoo \u003cem\u003ebar\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Indefinite levels of nesting are possible:","","```````````````````````````````` example","**foo *bar **baz**","bim* bop**",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003efoo \u003cem\u003ebar \u003cstrong\u003ebaz\u003c/strong\u003e","bim\u003c/em\u003e bop\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","**foo [*bar*](/url)**",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003efoo \u003ca href=\"/url\"\u003e\u003cem\u003ebar\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","There can be no empty emphasis or strong emphasis:","","```````````````````````````````` example","__ is not an empty emphasis",".","\u003cp\u003e__ is not an empty emphasis\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","____ is not an empty strong emphasis",".","\u003cp\u003e____ is not an empty strong emphasis\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","","Rule 11:","","```````````````````````````````` example","foo ***",".","\u003cp\u003efoo ***\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","foo *\\**",".","\u003cp\u003efoo \u003cem\u003e*\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","foo *_*",".","\u003cp\u003efoo \u003cem\u003e_\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","foo *****",".","\u003cp\u003efoo *****\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","foo **\\***",".","\u003cp\u003efoo \u003cstrong\u003e*\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","foo **_**",".","\u003cp\u003efoo \u003cstrong\u003e_\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Note that when delimiters do not match evenly, Rule 11 determines","that the excess literal `*` characters will appear outside of the","emphasis, rather than inside it:","","```````````````````````````````` example","**foo*",".","\u003cp\u003e*\u003cem\u003efoo\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","*foo**",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cem\u003efoo\u003c/em\u003e*\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","***foo**",".","\u003cp\u003e*\u003cstrong\u003efoo\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","****foo*",".","\u003cp\u003e***\u003cem\u003efoo\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","**foo***",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003efoo\u003c/strong\u003e*\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","*foo****",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cem\u003efoo\u003c/em\u003e***\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","","Rule 12:","","```````````````````````````````` example","foo ___",".","\u003cp\u003efoo ___\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","foo _\\__",".","\u003cp\u003efoo \u003cem\u003e_\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","foo _*_",".","\u003cp\u003efoo \u003cem\u003e*\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","foo _____",".","\u003cp\u003efoo
