\u003cstrong\u003e*\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","__foo_",".","\u003cp\u003e_\u003cem\u003efoo\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Note that when delimiters do not match evenly, Rule 12 determines","that the excess literal `_` characters will appear outside of the","emphasis, rather than inside it:","","```````````````````````````````` example","_foo__",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cem\u003efoo\u003c/em\u003e_\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","___foo__",".","\u003cp\u003e_\u003cstrong\u003efoo\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","____foo_",".","\u003cp\u003e___\u003cem\u003efoo\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","__foo___",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003efoo\u003c/strong\u003e_\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","_foo____",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cem\u003efoo\u003c/em\u003e___\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Rule 13 implies that if you want emphasis nested directly inside","emphasis, you must use different delimiters:","","```````````````````````````````` example","**foo**",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003efoo\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","*_foo_*",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cem\u003e\u003cem\u003efoo\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","__foo__",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003efoo\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","_*foo*_",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cem\u003e\u003cem\u003efoo\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","However, strong emphasis within strong emphasis is possible without","switching delimiters:","","```````````````````````````````` example","****foo****",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e\u003cstrong\u003efoo\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","____foo____",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e\u003cstrong\u003efoo\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","","Rule 13 can be applied to arbitrarily long sequences of","delimiters:","","```````````````````````````````` example","******foo******",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e\u003cstrong\u003efoo\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Rule 14:","","```````````````````````````````` example","***foo***",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cem\u003e\u003cstrong\u003efoo\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","_____foo_____",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cem\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e\u003cstrong\u003efoo\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Rule 15:","","```````````````````````````````` example","*foo _bar* baz_",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cem\u003efoo _bar\u003c/em\u003e baz_\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","*foo __bar *baz bim__ bam*",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cem\u003efoo \u003cstrong\u003ebar *baz bim\u003c/strong\u003e bam\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Rule 16:","","```````````````````````````````` example","**foo **bar baz**",".","\u003cp\u003e**foo \u003cstrong\u003ebar baz\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","*foo *bar baz*",".","\u003cp\u003e*foo \u003cem\u003ebar baz\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Rule 17:","","```````````````````````````````` example","*[bar*](/url)",".","\u003cp\u003e*\u003ca href=\"/url\"\u003ebar*\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","_foo [bar_](/url)",".","\u003cp\u003e_foo \u003ca href=\"/url\"\u003ebar_\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","*\u003cimg src=\"foo\" title=\"*\"/\u003e",".","\u003cp\u003e*\u003cimg src=\"foo\" title=\"*\"/\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","**\u003ca href=\"**\"\u003e",".","\u003cp\u003e**\u003ca href=\"**\"\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","__\u003ca href=\"__\"\u003e",".","\u003cp\u003e__\u003ca href=\"__\"\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","*a `*`*",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cem\u003ea \u003ccode\u003e*\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","_a `_`_",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cem\u003ea \u003ccode\u003e_\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","**a\u003chttps://foo.bar/?q=**\u003e",".","\u003cp\u003e**a\u003ca href=\"https://foo.bar/?q=**\"\u003ehttps://foo.bar/?q=**\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","__a\u003chttps://foo.bar/?q=__\u003e",".","\u003cp\u003e__a\u003ca href=\"https://foo.bar/?q=__\"\u003ehttps://foo.bar/?q=__\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","","## Links","","A link contains [link text] (the visible text), a [link destination]","(the URI that is the link destination), and optionally a [link title].","There are two basic kinds of links in Markdown.  In [inline links] the","destination and title are given immediately after the link text.  In","[reference links] the destination and title are defined elsewhere in","the document.","","A [link text](@) consists of a sequence of zero or more","inline elements enclosed by square brackets (`[` and `]`).  The","following rules apply:","","- Links may not contain other links, at any level of nesting. If","  multiple otherwise valid link definitions appear nested inside each","  other, the inner-most definition is used.","","- Brackets are allowed in the [link text] only if (a) they","  are backslash-escaped or (b) they appear as a matched pair of brackets,","  with an open bracket `[`, a sequence of zero or more inlines, and","  a close bracket `]`.","","- Backtick [code spans], [autolinks], and raw [HTML tags] bind more tightly","  than the brackets in link text.  Thus, for example,","  `` [foo`]` `` could not be a link text, since the second `]`","  is part of a code span.","","- The brackets in link text bind more tightly than markers for","  [emphasis and strong emphasis]. Thus, for example, `*[foo*](url)` is a link.","","A [link destination](@) consists of either","","- a sequence of zero or more characters between an opening `\u003c` and a","  closing `\u003e` that contains no line endings or unescaped","  `\u003c` or `\u003e` characters, or","","- a nonempty sequence of characters that does not start with `\u003c`,","  does not include [ASCII control characters][ASCII control character]","  or [space] character, and includes parentheses only if (a) they are","  backslash-escaped or (b) they are part of a balanced pair of","  unescaped parentheses.","  (Implementations may impose limits on parentheses nesting to","  avoid performance issues, but at least three levels of nesting","  should be supported.)","","A [link title](@)  consists of either","","- a sequence of zero or more characters between straight double-quote","  characters (`\"`), including a `\"` character only if it is","  backslash-escaped, or","","- a sequence of zero or more characters between straight single-quote","  characters (`'`), including a `'` character only if it is","  backslash-escaped, or","","- a sequence of zero or more characters between matching parentheses","  (`(...)`), including a `(` or `)` character only if it is","  backslash-escaped.","","Although [link titles] may span multiple lines, they may not contain","a [blank line].","","An [inline link](@) consists of a [link text] followed immediately","by a left parenthesis `(`, an optional [link destination], an optional","[link title], and a right parenthesis `)`.","These four components may be separated by spaces, tabs, and up to one line","ending.","If both [link destination] and [link title] are present, they *must* be","separated by spaces, tabs, and up to one line ending.","","The link's text consists of the inlines contained","in the [link text] (excluding the enclosing square brackets).","The link's URI consists of the link destination, excluding enclosing","`\u003c...\u003e` if present, with backslash-escapes in effect as described","above.  The link's title consists of the link title, excluding its","enclosing delimiters, with backslash-escapes in effect as described","above.","","Here is a simple inline link:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[link](/uri \"title\")",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"/uri\" title=\"title\"\u003elink\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","The title, the link text and even ","the destination may be omitted:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[link](/uri)",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"/uri\"\u003elink\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","```````````````````````````````` example","[](./target.md)",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"./target.md\"\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","[link]()",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"\"\u003elink\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","[link](\u003c\u003e)",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"\"\u003elink\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","[]()",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"\"\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","The destination can only contain spaces if it is","enclosed in pointy brackets:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[link](/my uri)",".","\u003cp\u003e[link](/my uri)\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","```````````````````````````````` example","[link](\u003c/my uri\u003e)",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"/my%20uri\"\u003elink\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","The destination cannot contain line endings,","even if enclosed in pointy brackets:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[link](foo","bar)",".","\u003cp\u003e[link](foo","bar)\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","```````````````````````````````` example","[link](\u003cfoo","bar\u003e)",".","\u003cp\u003e[link](\u003cfoo","bar\u003e)\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","The destination can contain `)` if it is enclosed","in pointy brackets:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[a](\u003cb)c\u003e)",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"b)c\"\u003ea\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","Pointy brackets that enclose links must be unescaped:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[link](\u003cfoo\\\u003e)",".","\u003cp\u003e[link](\u0026lt;foo\u0026gt;)\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","These are not links, because the opening pointy bracket","is not matched properly:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[a](\u003cb)c","[a](\u003cb)c\u003e","[a](\u003cb\u003ec)",".","\u003cp\u003e[a](\u0026lt;b)c","[a](\u0026lt;b)c\u0026gt;","[a](\u003cb\u003ec)\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","Parentheses inside the link destination may be escaped:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[link](\\(foo\\))",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"(foo)\"\u003elink\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","Any number of parentheses are allowed without escaping, as long as they are","balanced:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[link](foo(and(bar)))",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"foo(and(bar))\"\u003elink\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","However, if you have unbalanced parentheses, you need to escape or use the","`\u003c...\u003e` form:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[link](foo(and(bar))",".","\u003cp\u003e[link](foo(and(bar))\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","[link](foo\\(and\\(bar\\))",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"foo(and(bar)\"\u003elink\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","[link](\u003cfoo(and(bar)\u003e)",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"foo(and(bar)\"\u003elink\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Parentheses and other symbols can also be escaped, as usual","in Markdown:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[link](foo\\)\\:)",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"foo):\"\u003elink\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","A link can contain fragment identifiers and queries:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[link](#fragment)","","[link](https://example.com#fragment)","","[link](https://example.com?foo=3#frag)",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"#fragment\"\u003elink\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"https://example.com#fragment\"\u003elink\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"https://example.com?foo=3#frag\"\u003elink\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Note that a backslash before a non-escapable character is","just a backslash:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[link](foo\\bar)",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"foo%5Cbar\"\u003elink\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","URL-escaping should be left alone inside the destination, as all","URL-escaped characters are also valid URL characters. Entity and","numerical character references in the destination will be parsed","into the corresponding Unicode code points, as usual.  These may","be optionally URL-escaped when written as HTML, but this spec","does not enforce any particular policy for rendering URLs in","HTML or other formats.  Renderers may make different decisions","about how to escape or normalize URLs in the output.","","```````````````````````````````` example","[link](foo%20b\u0026auml;)",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"foo%20b%C3%A4\"\u003elink\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Note that, because titles can often be parsed as destinations,","if you try to omit the destination and keep the title, you'll","get unexpected results:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[link](\"title\")",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"%22title%22\"\u003elink\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Titles may be in single quotes, double quotes, or parentheses:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[link](/url \"title\")","[link](/url 'title')","[link](/url (title))",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"/url\" title=\"title\"\u003elink\u003c/a\u003e","\u003ca href=\"/url\" title=\"title\"\u003elink\u003c/a\u003e","\u003ca href=\"/url\" title=\"title\"\u003elink\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Backslash escapes and entity and numeric character references","may be used in titles:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[link](/url \"title \\\"\u0026quot;\")",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"/url\" title=\"title \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\"\u003elink\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Titles must be separated from the link using spaces, tabs, and up to one line","ending.","Other [Unicode whitespace] like non-breaking space doesn't work.","","```````````````````````````````` example","[link](/url \"title\")",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"/url%C2%A0%22title%22\"\u003elink\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Nested balanced quotes are not allowed without escaping:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[link](/url \"title \"and\" title\")",".","\u003cp\u003e[link](/url \u0026quot;title \u0026quot;and\u0026quot; title\u0026quot;)\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","But it is easy to work around this by using a different quote type:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[link](/url 'title \"and\" title')",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"/url\" title=\"title \u0026quot;and\u0026quot; title\"\u003elink\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","(Note:  `Markdown.pl` did allow double quotes inside a double-quoted","title, and its test suite included a test demonstrating this.","But it is hard to see a good rationale for the extra complexity this","brings, since there are already many ways---backslash escaping,","entity and numeric character references, or using a different","quote type for the enclosing title---to write titles containing","double quotes.  `Markdown.pl`'s handling of titles has a number","of other strange features.  For example, it allows single-quoted","titles in inline links, but not reference links.  And, in","reference links but not inline links, it allows a title to begin","with `\"` and end with `)`.  `Markdown.pl` 1.0.1 even allows","titles with no closing quotation mark, though 1.0.2b8 does not.","It seems preferable to adopt a simple, rational rule that works","the same way in inline links and link reference definitions.)","","Spaces, tabs, and up to one line ending is allowed around the destination and","title:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[link](   /uri","  \"title\"  )",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"/uri\" title=\"title\"\u003elink\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","But it is not allowed between the link text and the","following parenthesis:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[link] (/uri)",".","\u003cp\u003e[link] (/uri)\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","The link text may contain balanced brackets, but not unbalanced ones,","unless they are escaped:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[link [foo [bar]]](/uri)",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"/uri\"\u003elink [foo [bar]]\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","[link] bar](/uri)",".","\u003cp\u003e[link] bar](/uri)\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","[link [bar](/uri)",".","\u003cp\u003e[link \u003ca href=\"/uri\"\u003ebar\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","[link \\[bar](/uri)",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"/uri\"\u003elink [bar\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","The link text may contain inline content:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[link *foo **bar** `#`*](/uri)",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"/uri\"\u003elink \u003cem\u003efoo \u003cstrong\u003ebar\u003c/strong\u003e \u003ccode\u003e#\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","[![moon](moon.jpg)](/uri)",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"/uri\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\"moon.jpg\" alt=\"moon\" /\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","However, links may not contain other links, at any level of nesting.","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo [bar](/uri)](/uri)",".","\u003cp\u003e[foo \u003ca href=\"/uri\"\u003ebar\u003c/a\u003e](/uri)\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo *[bar [baz](/uri)](/uri)*](/uri)",".","\u003cp\u003e[foo \u003cem\u003e[bar \u003ca href=\"/uri\"\u003ebaz\u003c/a\u003e](/uri)\u003c/em\u003e](/uri)\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","![[[foo](uri1)](uri2)](uri3)",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cimg src=\"uri3\" alt=\"[foo](uri2)\" /\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","These cases illustrate the precedence of link text grouping over","emphasis grouping:","","```````````````````````````````` example","*[foo*](/uri)",".","\u003cp\u003e*\u003ca href=\"/uri\"\u003efoo*\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo *bar](baz*)",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"baz*\"\u003efoo *bar\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Note that brackets that *aren't* part of links do not take","precedence:","","```````````````````````````````` example","*foo [bar* baz]",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cem\u003efoo [bar\u003c/em\u003e baz]\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","These cases illustrate the precedence of HTML tags, code spans,","and autolinks over link grouping:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo \u003cbar attr=\"](baz)\"\u003e",".","\u003cp\u003e[foo \u003cbar attr=\"](baz)\"\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo`](/uri)`",".","\u003cp\u003e[foo\u003ccode\u003e](/uri)\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo\u003chttps://example.com/?search=](uri)\u003e",".","\u003cp\u003e[foo\u003ca href=\"https://example.com/?search=%5D(uri)\"\u003ehttps://example.com/?search=](uri)\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","There are three kinds of [reference link](@)s:","[full](#full-reference-link), [collapsed](#collapsed-reference-link),","and [shortcut](#shortcut-reference-link).","","A [full reference link](@)","consists of a [link text] immediately followed by a [link label]","that [matches] a [link reference definition] elsewhere in the document.","","A [link label](@)  begins with a left bracket (`[`) and ends","with the first right bracket (`]`) that is not backslash-escaped.","Between these brackets there must be at least one character that is not a space,","tab, or line ending.","Unescaped square bracket characters are not allowed inside the","opening and closing square brackets of [link labels].  A link","label can have at most 999 characters inside the square","brackets.","","One label [matches](@)","another just in case their normalized forms are equal.  To normalize a","label, strip off the opening and closing brackets,","perform the *Unicode case fold*, strip leading and trailing","spaces, tabs, and line endings, and collapse consecutive internal","spaces, tabs, and line endings to a single space.  If there are multiple","matching reference link definitions, the one that comes first in the","document is used.  (It is desirable in such cases to emit a warning.)","","The link's URI and title are provided by the matching [link","reference definition].","","Here is a simple example:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo][bar]","","[bar]: /url \"title\"",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"/url\" title=\"title\"\u003efoo\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","The rules for the [link text] are the same as with","[inline links].  Thus:","","The link text may contain balanced brackets, but not unbalanced ones,","unless they are escaped:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[link [foo [bar]]][ref]","","[ref]: /uri",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"/uri\"\u003elink [foo [bar]]\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","[link \\[bar][ref]","","[ref]: /uri",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"/uri\"\u003elink [bar\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","The link text may contain inline content:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[link *foo **bar** `#`*][ref]","","[ref]: /uri",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"/uri\"\u003elink \u003cem\u003efoo \u003cstrong\u003ebar\u003c/strong\u003e \u003ccode\u003e#\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","[![moon](moon.jpg)][ref]","","[ref]: /uri",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"/uri\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\"moon.jpg\" alt=\"moon\" /\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","However, links may not contain other links, at any level of nesting.","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo [bar](/uri)][ref]","","[ref]: /uri",".","\u003cp\u003e[foo \u003ca href=\"/uri\"\u003ebar\u003c/a\u003e]\u003ca href=\"/uri\"\u003eref\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo *bar [baz][ref]*][ref]","","[ref]: /uri",".","\u003cp\u003e[foo \u003cem\u003ebar \u003ca href=\"/uri\"\u003ebaz\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/em\u003e]\u003ca href=\"/uri\"\u003eref\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","(In the examples above, we have two [shortcut reference links]","instead of one [full reference link].)","","The following cases illustrate the precedence of link text grouping over","emphasis grouping:","","```````````````````````````````` example","*[foo*][ref]","","[ref]: /uri",".","\u003cp\u003e*\u003ca href=\"/uri\"\u003efoo*\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo *bar][ref]*","","[ref]: /uri",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"/uri\"\u003efoo *bar\u003c/a\u003e*\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","These cases illustrate the precedence of HTML tags, code spans,","and autolinks over link grouping:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo \u003cbar attr=\"][ref]\"\u003e","","[ref]: /uri",".","\u003cp\u003e[foo \u003cbar attr=\"][ref]\"\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo`][ref]`","","[ref]: /uri",".","\u003cp\u003e[foo\u003ccode\u003e][ref]\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo\u003chttps://example.com/?search=][ref]\u003e","","[ref]: /uri",".","\u003cp\u003e[foo\u003ca href=\"https://example.com/?search=%5D%5Bref%5D\"\u003ehttps://example.com/?search=][ref]\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Matching is case-insensitive:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo][BaR]","","[bar]: /url \"title\"",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"/url\" title=\"title\"\u003efoo\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Unicode case fold is used:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[ẞ]","","[SS]: /url",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"/url\"\u003eẞ\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Consecutive internal spaces, tabs, and line endings are treated as one space for","purposes of determining matching:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[Foo","  bar]: /url","","[Baz][Foo bar]",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"/url\"\u003eBaz\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","No spaces, tabs, or line endings are allowed between the [link text] and the","[link label]:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo] [bar]","","[bar]: /url \"title\"",".","\u003cp\u003e[foo] \u003ca href=\"/url\" title=\"title\"\u003ebar\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo]","[bar]","","[bar]: /url \"title\"",".","\u003cp\u003e[foo]","\u003ca href=\"/url\" title=\"title\"\u003ebar\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","This is a departure from John Gruber's original Markdown syntax","description, which explicitly allows whitespace between the link","text and the link label.  It brings reference links in line with","[inline links], which (according to both original Markdown and","this spec) cannot have whitespace after the link text.  More","importantly, it prevents inadvertent capture of consecutive","[shortcut reference links]. If whitespace is allowed between the","link text and the link label, then in the following we will have","a single reference link, not two shortcut reference links, as","intended:","","``` markdown","[foo]","[bar]","","[foo]: /url1","[bar]: /url2","```","","(Note that [shortcut reference links] were introduced by Gruber","himself in a beta version of `Markdown.pl`, but never included","in the official syntax description.  Without shortcut reference","links, it is harmless to allow space between the link text and","link label; but once shortcut references are introduced, it is","too dangerous to allow this, as it frequently leads to","unintended results.)","","When there are multiple matching [link reference definitions],","the first is used:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo]: /url1","","[foo]: /url2","","[bar][foo]",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"/url1\"\u003ebar\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Note that matching is performed on normalized strings, not parsed","inline content.  So the following does not match, even though the","labels define equivalent inline content:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[bar][foo\\!]","","[foo!]: /url",".","\u003cp\u003e[bar][foo!]\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","[Link labels] cannot contain brackets, unless they are","backslash-escaped:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo][ref[]","","[ref[]: /uri",".","\u003cp\u003e[foo][ref[]\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cp\u003e[ref[]: /uri\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo][ref[bar]]","","[ref[bar]]: /uri",".","\u003cp\u003e[foo][ref[bar]]\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cp\u003e[ref[bar]]: /uri\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","[[[foo]]]","","[[[foo]]]: /url",".","\u003cp\u003e[[[foo]]]\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cp\u003e[[[foo]]]: /url\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo][ref\\[]","","[ref\\[]: /uri",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"/uri\"\u003efoo\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Note that in this example `]` is not backslash-escaped:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[bar\\\\]: /uri","","[bar\\\\]",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"/uri\"\u003ebar\\\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","A [link label] must contain at least one character that is not a space, tab, or","line ending:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[]","","[]: /uri",".","\u003cp\u003e[]\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cp\u003e[]: /uri\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","["," ]","","["," ]: /uri",".","\u003cp\u003e[","]\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cp\u003e[","]: /uri\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","A [collapsed reference link](@)","consists of a [link label] that [matches] a","[link reference definition] elsewhere in the","document, followed by the string `[]`.","The contents of the link label are parsed as inlines,","which are used as the link's text.  The link's URI and title are","provided by the matching reference link definition.  Thus,","`[foo][]` is equivalent to `[foo][foo]`.","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo][]","","[foo]: /url \"title\"",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"/url\" title=\"title\"\u003efoo\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","[*foo* bar][]","","[*foo* bar]: /url \"title\"",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"/url\" title=\"title\"\u003e\u003cem\u003efoo\u003c/em\u003e bar\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","The link labels are case-insensitive:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[Foo][]","","[foo]: /url \"title\"",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"/url\" title=\"title\"\u003eFoo\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","","As with full reference links, spaces, tabs, or line endings are not","allowed between the two sets of brackets:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo] ","[]","","[foo]: /url \"title\"",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"/url\" title=\"title\"\u003efoo\u003c/a\u003e","[]\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","A [shortcut reference link](@)","consists of a [link label] that [matches] a","[link reference definition] elsewhere in the","document and is not followed by `[]` or a link label.","The contents of the link label are parsed as inlines,","which are used as the link's text.  The link's URI and title","are provided by the matching link reference definition.","Thus, `[foo]` is equivalent to `[foo][]`.","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo]","","[foo]: /url \"title\"",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"/url\" title=\"title\"\u003efoo\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","[*foo* bar]","","[*foo* bar]: /url \"title\"",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"/url\" title=\"title\"\u003e\u003cem\u003efoo\u003c/em\u003e bar\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","[[*foo* bar]]","","[*foo* bar]: /url \"title\"",".","\u003cp\u003e[\u003ca href=\"/url\" title=\"title\"\u003e\u003cem\u003efoo\u003c/em\u003e bar\u003c/a\u003e]\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","[[bar [foo]","","[foo]: /url",".","\u003cp\u003e[[bar \u003ca href=\"/url\"\u003efoo\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","The link labels are case-insensitive:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[Foo]","","[foo]: /url \"title\"",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"/url\" title=\"title\"\u003eFoo\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","A space after the link text should be preserved:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo] bar","","[foo]: /url",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"/url\"\u003efoo\u003c/a\u003e bar\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","If you just want bracketed text, you can backslash-escape the","opening bracket to avoid links:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\\[foo]","","[foo]: /url \"title\"",".","\u003cp\u003e[foo]\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Note that this is a link, because a link label ends with the first","following closing bracket:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo*]: /url","","*[foo*]",".","\u003cp\u003e*\u003ca href=\"/url\"\u003efoo*\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Full and collapsed references take precedence over shortcut","references:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo][bar]","","[foo]: /url1","[bar]: /url2",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"/url2\"\u003efoo\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo][]","","[foo]: /url1",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"/url1\"\u003efoo\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","Inline links also take precedence:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo]()","","[foo]: /url1",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"\"\u003efoo\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo](not a link)","","[foo]: /url1",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"/url1\"\u003efoo\u003c/a\u003e(not a link)\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","In the following case `[bar][baz]` is parsed as a reference,","`[foo]` as normal text:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo][bar][baz]","","[baz]: /url",".","\u003cp\u003e[foo]\u003ca href=\"/url\"\u003ebar\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Here, though, `[foo][bar]` is parsed as a reference, since","`[bar]` is defined:","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo][bar][baz]","","[baz]: /url1","[bar]: /url2",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"/url2\"\u003efoo\u003c/a\u003e\u003ca href=\"/url1\"\u003ebaz\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Here `[foo]` is not parsed as a shortcut reference, because it","is followed by a link label (even though `[bar]` is not defined):","","```````````````````````````````` example","[foo][bar][baz]","","[baz]: /url1","[foo]: /url2",".","\u003cp\u003e[foo]\u003ca href=\"/url1\"\u003ebar\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","","## Images","","Syntax for images is like the syntax for links, with one","difference. Instead of [link text], we have an","[image description](@).  The rules for this are the","same as for [link text], except that (a) an","image description starts with `![` rather than `[`, and","(b) an image description may contain links.","An image description has inline elements","as its contents.  When an image is rendered to HTML,","this is standardly used as the image's `alt` attribute.","","```````````````````````````````` example","![foo](/url \"title\")",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cimg src=\"/url\" alt=\"foo\" title=\"title\" /\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","![foo *bar*]","","[foo *bar*]: train.jpg \"train \u0026 tracks\"",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cimg src=\"train.jpg\" alt=\"foo bar\" title=\"train \u0026amp; tracks\" /\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","![foo ![bar](/url)](/url2)",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cimg src=\"/url2\" alt=\"foo bar\" /\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","![foo [bar](/url)](/url2)",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cimg src=\"/url2\" alt=\"foo bar\" /\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Though this spec is concerned with parsing, not rendering, it is","recommended that in rendering to HTML, only the plain string content","of the [image description] be used.  Note that in","the above example, the alt attribute's value is `foo bar`, not `foo","[bar](/url)` or `foo \u003ca href=\"/url\"\u003ebar\u003c/a\u003e`.  Only the plain string","content is rendered, without formatting.","","```````````````````````````````` example","![foo *bar*][]","","[foo *bar*]: train.jpg \"train \u0026 tracks\"",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cimg src=\"train.jpg\" alt=\"foo bar\" title=\"train \u0026amp; tracks\" /\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","![foo *bar*][foobar]","","[FOOBAR]: train.jpg \"train \u0026 tracks\"",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cimg src=\"train.jpg\" alt=\"foo bar\" title=\"train \u0026amp; tracks\" /\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","![foo](train.jpg)",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cimg src=\"train.jpg\" alt=\"foo\" /\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","My ![foo bar](/path/to/train.jpg  \"title\"   )",".","\u003cp\u003eMy \u003cimg src=\"/path/to/train.jpg\" alt=\"foo bar\" title=\"title\" /\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","![foo](\u003curl\u003e)",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cimg src=\"url\" alt=\"foo\" /\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","![](/url)",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cimg src=\"/url\" alt=\"\" /\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Reference-style:","","```````````````````````````````` example","![foo][bar]","","[bar]: /url",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cimg src=\"/url\" alt=\"foo\" /\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","![foo][bar]","","[BAR]: /url",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cimg src=\"/url\" alt=\"foo\" /\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Collapsed:","","```````````````````````````````` example","![foo][]","","[foo]: /url \"title\"",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cimg src=\"/url\" alt=\"foo\" title=\"title\" /\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","![*foo* bar][]","","[*foo* bar]: /url \"title\"",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cimg src=\"/url\" alt=\"foo bar\" title=\"title\" /\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","The labels are case-insensitive:","","```````````````````````````````` example","![Foo][]","","[foo]: /url \"title\"",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cimg src=\"/url\" alt=\"Foo\" title=\"title\" /\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","As with reference links, spaces, tabs, and line endings, are not allowed","between the two sets of brackets:","","```````````````````````````````` example","![foo] ","[]","","[foo]: /url \"title\"",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cimg src=\"/url\" alt=\"foo\" title=\"title\" /\u003e","[]\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Shortcut:","","```````````````````````````````` example","![foo]","","[foo]: /url \"title\"",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cimg src=\"/url\" alt=\"foo\" title=\"title\" /\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","![*foo* bar]","","[*foo* bar]: /url \"title\"",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cimg src=\"/url\" alt=\"foo bar\" title=\"title\" /\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Note that link labels cannot contain unescaped brackets:","","```````````````````````````````` example","![[foo]]","","[[foo]]: /url \"title\"",".","\u003cp\u003e![[foo]]\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cp\u003e[[foo]]: /url \u0026quot;title\u0026quot;\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","The link labels are case-insensitive:","","```````````````````````````````` example","![Foo]","","[foo]: /url \"title\"",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cimg src=\"/url\" alt=\"Foo\" title=\"title\" /\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","If you just want a literal `!` followed by bracketed text, you can","backslash-escape the opening `[`:","","```````````````````````````````` example","!\\[foo]","","[foo]: /url \"title\"",".","\u003cp\u003e![foo]\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","If you want a link after a literal `!`, backslash-escape the","`!`:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\\![foo]","","[foo]: /url \"title\"",".","\u003cp\u003e!\u003ca href=\"/url\" title=\"title\"\u003efoo\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","## Autolinks","","[Autolink](@)s are absolute URIs and email addresses inside","`\u003c` and `\u003e`. They are parsed as links, with the URL or email address","as the link label.","","A [URI autolink](@) consists of `\u003c`, followed by an","[absolute URI] followed by `\u003e`.  It is parsed as","a link to the URI, with the URI as the link's label.","","An [absolute URI](@),","for these purposes, consists of a [scheme] followed by a colon (`:`)","followed by zero or more characters other than [ASCII control","characters][ASCII control character], [space], `\u003c`, and `\u003e`.","If the URI includes these characters, they must be percent-encoded","(e.g. `%20` for a space).","","For purposes of this spec, a [scheme](@) is any sequence","of 2--32 characters beginning with an ASCII letter and followed","by any combination of ASCII letters, digits, or the symbols plus","(\"+\"), period (\".\"), or hyphen (\"-\").","","Here are some valid autolinks:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003chttp://foo.bar.baz\u003e",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"http://foo.bar.baz\"\u003ehttp://foo.bar.baz\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003chttps://foo.bar.baz/test?q=hello\u0026id=22\u0026boolean\u003e",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"https://foo.bar.baz/test?q=hello\u0026amp;id=22\u0026amp;boolean\"\u003ehttps://foo.bar.baz/test?q=hello\u0026amp;id=22\u0026amp;boolean\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003circ://foo.bar:2233/baz\u003e",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"irc://foo.bar:2233/baz\"\u003eirc://foo.bar:2233/baz\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Uppercase is also fine:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003cMAILTO:FOO@BAR.BAZ\u003e",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"MAILTO:FOO@BAR.BAZ\"\u003eMAILTO:FOO@BAR.BAZ\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Note that many strings that count as [absolute URIs] for","purposes of this spec are not valid URIs, because their","schemes are not registered or because of other problems","with their syntax:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003ca+b+c:d\u003e",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"a+b+c:d\"\u003ea+b+c:d\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003cmade-up-scheme://foo,bar\u003e",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"made-up-scheme://foo,bar\"\u003emade-up-scheme://foo,bar\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003chttps://../\u003e",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"https://../\"\u003ehttps://../\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003clocalhost:5001/foo\u003e",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"localhost:5001/foo\"\u003elocalhost:5001/foo\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Spaces are not allowed in autolinks:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003chttps://foo.bar/baz bim\u003e",".","\u003cp\u003e\u0026lt;https://foo.bar/baz bim\u0026gt;\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Backslash-escapes do not work inside autolinks:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003chttps://example.com/\\[\\\u003e",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"https://example.com/%5C%5B%5C\"\u003ehttps://example.com/\\[\\\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","An [email autolink](@)","consists of `\u003c`, followed by an [email address],","followed by `\u003e`.  The link's label is the email address,","and the URL is `mailto:` followed by the email address.","","An [email address](@),","for these purposes, is anything that matches","the [non-normative regex from the HTML5","spec](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/forms.html#e-mail-state-(type=email)):","","    /^[a-zA-Z0-9.!#$%\u0026'*+/=?^_`{|}~-]+@[a-zA-Z0-9](?:[a-zA-Z0-9-]{0,61}[a-zA-Z0-9])?","    (?:\\.[a-zA-Z0-9](?:[a-zA-Z0-9-]{0,61}[a-zA-Z0-9])?)*$/","","Examples of email autolinks:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003cfoo@bar.example.com\u003e",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"mailto:foo@bar.example.com\"\u003efoo@bar.example.com\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003cfoo+special@Bar.baz-bar0.com\u003e",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"mailto:foo+special@Bar.baz-bar0.com\"\u003efoo+special@Bar.baz-bar0.com\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Backslash-escapes do not work inside email autolinks:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003cfoo\\+@bar.example.com\u003e",".","\u003cp\u003e\u0026lt;foo+@bar.example.com\u0026gt;\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","These are not autolinks:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003c\u003e",".","\u003cp\u003e\u0026lt;\u0026gt;\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003c https://foo.bar \u003e",".","\u003cp\u003e\u0026lt; https://foo.bar \u0026gt;\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003cm:abc\u003e",".","\u003cp\u003e\u0026lt;m:abc\u0026gt;\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003cfoo.bar.baz\u003e",".","\u003cp\u003e\u0026lt;foo.bar.baz\u0026gt;\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","https://example.com",".","\u003cp\u003ehttps://example.com\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","foo@bar.example.com",".","\u003cp\u003efoo@bar.example.com\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","## Raw HTML","","Text between `\u003c` and `\u003e` that looks like an HTML tag is parsed as a","raw HTML tag and will be rendered in HTML without escaping.","Tag and attribute names are not limited to current HTML tags,","so custom tags (and even, say, DocBook tags) may be used.","","Here is the grammar for tags:","","A [tag name](@) consists of an ASCII letter","followed by zero or more ASCII letters, digits, or","hyphens (`-`).","","An [attribute](@) consists of spaces, tabs, and up to one line ending,","an [attribute name], and an optional","[attribute value specification].","","An [attribute name](@)","consists of an ASCII letter, `_`, or `:`, followed by zero or more ASCII","letters, digits, `_`, `.`, `:`, or `-`.  (Note:  This is the XML","specification restricted to ASCII.  HTML5 is laxer.)","","An [attribute value specification](@)","consists of optional spaces, tabs, and up to one line ending,","a `=` character, optional spaces, tabs, and up to one line ending,","and an [attribute value].","","An [attribute value](@)","consists of an [unquoted attribute value],","a [single-quoted attribute value], or a [double-quoted attribute value].","","An [unquoted attribute value](@)","is a nonempty string of characters not","including spaces, tabs, line endings, `\"`, `'`, `=`, `\u003c`, `\u003e`, or `` ` ``.","","A [single-quoted attribute value](@)","consists of `'`, zero or more","characters not including `'`, and a final `'`.","","A [double-quoted attribute value](@)","consists of `\"`, zero or more","characters not including `\"`, and a final `\"`.","","An [open tag](@) consists of a `\u003c` character, a [tag name],","zero or more [attributes], optional spaces, tabs, and up to one line ending,","an optional `/` character, and a `\u003e` character.","","A [closing tag](@) consists of the string `\u003c/`, a","[tag name], optional spaces, tabs, and up to one line ending, and the character","`\u003e`.","","An [HTML comment](@) consists of `\u003c!--\u003e`, `\u003c!---\u003e`, or  `\u003c!--`, a string of","characters not including the string `--\u003e`, and `--\u003e` (see the","[HTML spec](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/parsing.html#markup-declaration-open-state)).","","A [processing instruction](@)","consists of the string `\u003c?`, a string","of characters not including the string `?\u003e`, and the string","`?\u003e`.","","A [declaration](@) consists of the string `\u003c!`, an ASCII letter, zero or more","characters not including the character `\u003e`, and the character `\u003e`.","","A [CDATA section](@) consists of","the string `\u003c![CDATA[`, a string of characters not including the string","`]]\u003e`, and the string `]]\u003e`.","","An [HTML tag](@) consists of an [open tag], a [closing tag],","an [HTML comment], a [processing instruction], a [declaration],","or a [CDATA section].","","Here are some simple open tags:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003ca\u003e\u003cbab\u003e\u003cc2c\u003e",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca\u003e\u003cbab\u003e\u003cc2c\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Empty elements:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003ca/\u003e\u003cb2/\u003e",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca/\u003e\u003cb2/\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Whitespace is allowed:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003ca  /\u003e\u003cb2","data=\"foo\" \u003e",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca  /\u003e\u003cb2","data=\"foo\" \u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","With attributes:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003ca foo=\"bar\" bam = 'baz \u003cem\u003e\"\u003c/em\u003e'","_boolean zoop:33=zoop:33 /\u003e",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca foo=\"bar\" bam = 'baz \u003cem\u003e\"\u003c/em\u003e'","_boolean zoop:33=zoop:33 /\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Custom tag names can be used:","","```````````````````````````````` example","Foo \u003cresponsive-image src=\"foo.jpg\" /\u003e",".","\u003cp\u003eFoo \u003cresponsive-image src=\"foo.jpg\" /\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Illegal tag names, not parsed as HTML:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003c33\u003e \u003c__\u003e",".","\u003cp\u003e\u0026lt;33\u0026gt; \u0026lt;__\u0026gt;\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Illegal attribute names:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003ca h*#ref=\"hi\"\u003e",".","\u003cp\u003e\u0026lt;a h*#ref=\u0026quot;hi\u0026quot;\u0026gt;\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Illegal attribute values:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003ca href=\"hi'\u003e \u003ca href=hi'\u003e",".","\u003cp\u003e\u0026lt;a href=\u0026quot;hi'\u0026gt; \u0026lt;a href=hi'\u0026gt;\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Illegal whitespace:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003c a\u003e\u003c","foo\u003e\u003cbar/ \u003e","\u003cfoo bar=baz","bim!bop /\u003e",".","\u003cp\u003e\u0026lt; a\u0026gt;\u0026lt;","foo\u0026gt;\u0026lt;bar/ \u0026gt;","\u0026lt;foo bar=baz","bim!bop /\u0026gt;\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Missing whitespace:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003ca href='bar'title=title\u003e",".","\u003cp\u003e\u0026lt;a href='bar'title=title\u0026gt;\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Closing tags:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/foo \u003e",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/foo \u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Illegal attributes in closing tag:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003c/a href=\"foo\"\u003e",".","\u003cp\u003e\u0026lt;/a href=\u0026quot;foo\u0026quot;\u0026gt;\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Comments:","","```````````````````````````````` example","foo \u003c!-- this is a --","comment - with hyphens --\u003e",".","\u003cp\u003efoo \u003c!-- this is a --","comment - with hyphens --\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","```````````````````````````````` example","foo \u003c!--\u003e foo --\u003e","","foo \u003c!---\u003e foo --\u003e",".","\u003cp\u003efoo \u003c!--\u003e foo --\u0026gt;\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cp\u003efoo \u003c!---\u003e foo --\u0026gt;\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Processing instructions:","","```````````````````````````````` example","foo \u003c?php echo $a; ?\u003e",".","\u003cp\u003efoo \u003c?php echo $a; ?\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Declarations:","","```````````````````````````````` example","foo \u003c!ELEMENT br EMPTY\u003e",".","\u003cp\u003efoo \u003c!ELEMENT br EMPTY\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","CDATA sections:","","```````````````````````````````` example","foo \u003c![CDATA[\u003e\u0026\u003c]]\u003e",".","\u003cp\u003efoo \u003c![CDATA[\u003e\u0026\u003c]]\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Entity and numeric character references are preserved in HTML","attributes:","","```````````````````````````````` example","foo \u003ca href=\"\u0026ouml;\"\u003e",".","\u003cp\u003efoo \u003ca href=\"\u0026ouml;\"\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Backslash escapes do not work in HTML attributes:","","```````````````````````````````` example","foo \u003ca href=\"\\*\"\u003e",".","\u003cp\u003efoo \u003ca href=\"\\*\"\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003ca href=\"\\\"\"\u003e",".","\u003cp\u003e\u0026lt;a href=\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026gt;\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","A block quote can prevent a line from being parsed as inline HTML,","even though line breaks are allowed in tags:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003ca","\u003e quoted text",".","\u003cp\u003e\u0026lt;a\u003c/p\u003e","\u003cblockquote\u003e","\u003cp\u003equoted text\u003c/p\u003e","\u003c/blockquote\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","## Hard line breaks","","A line ending (not in a code span or HTML tag) that is preceded","by two or more spaces and does not occur at the end of a block","is parsed as a [hard line break](@) (rendered","in HTML as a `\u003cbr /\u003e` tag):","","```````````````````````````````` example","foo  ","baz",".","\u003cp\u003efoo\u003cbr /\u003e","baz\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","For a more visible alternative, a backslash before the","[line ending] may be used instead of two or more spaces:","","```````````````````````````````` example","foo\\","baz",".","\u003cp\u003efoo\u003cbr /\u003e","baz\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","More than two spaces can be used:","","```````````````````````````````` example","foo       ","baz",".","\u003cp\u003efoo\u003cbr /\u003e","baz\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Leading spaces at the beginning of the next line are ignored:","","```````````````````````````````` example","foo  ","     bar",".","\u003cp\u003efoo\u003cbr /\u003e","bar\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","foo\\","     bar",".","\u003cp\u003efoo\u003cbr /\u003e","bar\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Hard line breaks can occur inside emphasis, links, and other constructs","that allow inline content:","","```````````````````````````````` example","*foo  ","bar*",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cem\u003efoo\u003cbr /\u003e","bar\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","*foo\\","bar*",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003cem\u003efoo\u003cbr /\u003e","bar\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Hard line breaks do not occur inside code spans","","```````````````````````````````` example","`code  ","span`",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ccode\u003ecode   span\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","`code\\","span`",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ccode\u003ecode\\ span\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","or HTML tags:","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003ca href=\"foo  ","bar\"\u003e",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"foo  ","bar\"\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","\u003ca href=\"foo\\","bar\"\u003e",".","\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"foo\\","bar\"\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Hard line breaks are for separating inline content within a block.","Neither syntax for hard line breaks works at the end of a paragraph or","other block element:","","```````````````````````````````` example","foo\\",".","\u003cp\u003efoo\\\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","foo  ",".","\u003cp\u003efoo\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","### foo\\",".","\u003ch3\u003efoo\\\u003c/h3\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","### foo  ",".","\u003ch3\u003efoo\u003c/h3\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","## Soft line breaks","","A regular line ending (not in a code span or HTML tag) that is not","preceded by two or more spaces or a backslash is parsed as a","[softbreak](@).  (A soft line break may be rendered in HTML either as a","[line ending] or as a space. The result will be the same in","browsers. In the examples here, a [line ending] will be used.)","","```````````````````````````````` example","foo","baz",".","\u003cp\u003efoo","baz\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Spaces at the end of the line and beginning of the next line are","removed:","","```````````````````````````````` example","foo "," baz",".","\u003cp\u003efoo","baz\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","A conforming parser may render a soft line break in HTML either as a","line ending or as a space.","","A renderer may also provide an option to render soft line breaks","as hard line breaks.","","## Textual content","","Any characters not given an interpretation by the above rules will","be parsed as plain textual content.","","```````````````````````````````` example","hello $.;'there",".","\u003cp\u003ehello $.;'there\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","```````````````````````````````` example","Foo χρῆν",".","\u003cp\u003eFoo χρῆν\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","Internal spaces are preserved verbatim:","","```````````````````````````````` example","Multiple     spaces",".","\u003cp\u003eMultiple     spaces\u003c/p\u003e","````````````````````````````````","","","\u003c!-- END TESTS --\u003e","","# Appendix: A parsing strategy","","In this appendix we describe some features of the parsing strategy","used in the CommonMark reference implementations.","","## Overview","","Parsing has two phases:","","1. In the first phase, lines of input are consumed and the block","structure of the document---its division into paragraphs, block quotes,","list items, and so on---is constructed.  Text is assigned to these","blocks but not parsed. Link reference definitions are parsed and a","map of links is constructed.","","2. In the second phase, the raw text contents of paragraphs and headings","are parsed into sequences of Markdown inline elements (strings,","code spans, links, emphasis, and so on), using the map of link","references constructed in phase 1.","","At each point in processing, the document is represented as a tree of","**blocks**.  The root of the tree is a `document` block.  The `document`","may have any number of other blocks as **children**.  These children","may, in turn, have other blocks as children.  The last child of a block","is normally considered **open**, meaning that subsequent lines of input","can alter its contents.  (Blocks that are not open are **closed**.)","Here, for example, is a possible document tree, with the open blocks","marked by arrows:","","``` tree","-\u003e document","  -\u003e block_quote","       paragraph","         \"Lorem ipsum dolor\\nsit amet.\"","    -\u003e list (type=bullet tight=true bullet_char=-)","         list_item","           paragraph","             \"Qui *quodsi iracundia*\"","      -\u003e list_item","        -\u003e paragraph","             \"aliquando id\"","```","","## Phase 1: block structure","","Each line that is processed has an effect on this tree.  The line is","analyzed and, depending on its contents, the document may be altered","in one or more of the following ways:","","1. One or more open blocks may be closed.","2. One or more new blocks may be created as children of the","   last open block.","3. Text may be added to the last (deepest) open block remaining","   on the tree.","","Once a line has been incorporated into the tree in this way,","it can be discarded, so input can be read in a stream.","","For each line, we follow this procedure:","","1. First we iterate through the open blocks, starting with the","root document, and descending through last children down to the last","open block.  Each block imposes a condition that the line must satisfy","if the block is to remain open.  For example, a block quote requires a","`\u003e` character.  A paragraph requires a non-blank line.","In this phase we may match all or just some of the open","blocks.  But we cannot close unmatched blocks yet, because we may have a","[lazy continuation line].","","2.  Next, after consuming the continuation markers for existing","blocks, we look for new block starts (e.g. `\u003e` for a block quote).","If we encounter a new block start, we close any blocks unmatched","in step 1 before creating the new block as a child of the last","matched container block.","","3.  Finally, we look at the remainder of the line (after block","markers like `\u003e`, list markers, and indentation have been consumed).","This is text that can be incorporated into the last open","block (a paragraph, code block, heading, or raw HTML).","","Setext headings are formed when we see a line of a paragraph","that is a [setext heading underline].","","Reference link definitions are detected when a paragraph is closed;","the accumulated text lines are parsed to see if they begin with","one or more reference link definitions.  Any remainder becomes a","normal paragraph.","","We can see how this works by considering how the tree above is","generated by four lines of Markdown:","","``` markdown","\u003e Lorem ipsum dolor","sit amet.","\u003e - Qui *quodsi iracundia*","\u003e - aliquando id","```","","At the outset, our document model is just","","``` tree","-\u003e document","```","","The first line of our text,","","``` markdown","\u003e Lorem ipsum dolor","```","","causes a `block_quote` block to be created as a child of our","open `document` block, and a `paragraph` block as a child of","the `block_quote`.  Then the text is added to the last open","block, the `paragraph`:","","``` tree","-\u003e document","  -\u003e block_quote","    -\u003e paragraph","         \"Lorem ipsum dolor\"","```","","The next line,","","``` markdown","sit amet.","```","","is a \"lazy continuation\" of the open `paragraph`, so it gets added","to the paragraph's text:","","``` tree","-\u003e document","  -\u003e block_quote","    -\u003e paragraph","         \"Lorem ipsum dolor\\nsit amet.\"","```","","The third line,","","``` markdown","\u003e - Qui *quodsi iracundia*","```","","causes the `paragraph` block to be closed, and a new `list` block","opened as a child of the `block_quote`.  A `list_item` is also","added as a child of the `list`, and a `paragraph` as a child of","the `list_item`.  The text is then added to the new `paragraph`:","","``` tree","-\u003e document","  -\u003e block_quote","       paragraph","         \"Lorem ipsum dolor\\nsit amet.\"","    -\u003e list (type=bullet tight=true bullet_char=-)","      -\u003e list_item","        -\u003e paragraph","             \"Qui *quodsi iracundia*\"","```","","The fourth line,","","``` markdown","\u003e - aliquando id","```","","causes the `list_item` (and its child the `paragraph`) to be closed,","and a new `list_item` opened up as child of the `list`.  A `paragraph`","is added as a child of the new `list_item`, to contain the text.","We thus obtain the final tree:","","``` tree","-\u003e document","  -\u003e block_quote","       paragraph","         \"Lorem ipsum dolor\\nsit amet.\"","    -\u003e list (type=bullet tight=true bullet_char=-)","         list_item","           paragraph","             \"Qui *quodsi iracundia*\"","      -\u003e list_item","        -\u003e paragraph","             \"aliquando id\"","```","","## Phase 2: inline structure","","Once all of the input has been parsed, all open blocks are closed.","","We then \"walk the tree,\" visiting every node, and parse raw","string contents of paragraphs and headings as inlines.  At this","point we have seen all the link reference definitions, so we can","resolve reference links as we go.","","``` tree","document","  block_quote","    paragraph","      str \"Lorem ipsum dolor\"","      softbreak","      str \"sit amet.\"","    list (type=bullet tight=true bullet_char=-)","      list_item","        paragraph","          str \"Qui \"","          emph","            str \"quodsi iracundia\"","      list_item","        paragraph","          str \"aliquando id\"","```","","Notice how the [line ending] in the first paragraph has","been parsed as a `softbreak`, and the asterisks in the first list item","have become an `emph`.","","### An algorithm for parsing nested emphasis and links","","By far the trickiest part of inline parsing is handling emphasis,","strong emphasis, links, and images.  This is done using the following","algorithm.","","When we're parsing inlines and we hit either","","- a run of `*` or `_` characters, or","- a `[` or `![`","","we insert a text node with these symbols as its literal content, and we","add a pointer to this text node to the [delimiter stack](@).","","The [delimiter stack] is a doubly linked list.  Each","element contains a pointer to a text node, plus information about","","- the type of delimiter (`[`, `![`, `*`, `_`)","- the number of delimiters,","- whether the delimiter is \"active\" (all are active to start), and","- whether the delimiter is a potential opener, a potential closer,","  or both (which depends on what sort of characters precede","  and follow the delimiters).","","When we hit a `]` character, we call the *look for link or image*","procedure (see below).","","When we hit the end of the input, we call the *process emphasis*","procedure (see below), with `stack_bottom` = NULL.","","#### *look for link or image*","","Starting at the top of the delimiter stack, we look backwards","through the stack for an opening `[` or `![` delimiter.","","- If we don't find one, we return a literal text node `]`.","","- If we do find one, but it's not *active*, we remove the inactive","  delimiter from the stack, and return a literal text node `]`.","","- If we find one and it's active, then we parse ahead to see if","  we have an inline link/image, reference link/image, collapsed reference","  link/image, or shortcut reference link/image.","","  + If we don't, then we remove the opening delimiter from the","    delimiter stack and return a literal text node `]`.","","  + If we do, then","","    * We return a link or image node whose children are the inlines","      after the text node pointed to by the opening delimiter.","","    * We run *process emphasis* on these inlines, with the `[` opener","      as `stack_bottom`.","","    * We remove the opening delimiter.","","    * If we have a link (and not an image), we also set all","      `[` delimiters before the opening delimiter to *inactive*.  (This","      will prevent us from getting links within links.)","","#### *process emphasis*","","Parameter `stack_bottom` sets a lower bound to how far we","descend in the [delimiter stack].  If it is NULL, we can","go all the way to the bottom.  Otherwise, we stop before","visiting `stack_bottom`.","","Let `current_position` point to the element on the [delimiter stack]","just above `stack_bottom` (or the first element if `stack_bottom`","is NULL).","","We keep track of the `openers_bottom` for each delimiter","type (`*`, `_`), indexed to the length of the closing delimiter run","(modulo 3) and to whether the closing delimiter can also be an","opener.  Initialize this to `stack_bottom`.","","Then we repeat the following until we run out of potential","closers:","","- Move `current_position` forward in the delimiter stack (if needed)","  until we find the first potential closer with delimiter `*` or `_`.","  (This will be the potential closer closest","  to the beginning of the input -- the first one in parse order.)","","- Now, look back in the stack (staying above `stack_bottom` and","  the `openers_bottom` for this delimiter type) for the","  first matching potential opener (\"matching\" means same delimiter).","","- If one is found:","","  + Figure out whether we have emphasis or strong emphasis:","    if both closer and opener spans have length \u003e= 2, we have","    strong, otherwise regular.","","  + Insert an emph or strong emph node accordingly, after","    the text node corresponding to the opener.","","  + Remove any delimiters between the opener and closer from","    the delimiter stack.","","  + Remove 1 (for regular emph) or 2 (for strong emph) delimiters","    from the opening and closing text nodes.  If they become empty","    as a result, remove them and remove the corresponding element","    of the delimiter stack.  If the closing node is removed, reset","    `current_position` to the next element in the stack.","","- If none is found:","","  + Set `openers_bottom` to the element before `current_position`.","    (We know that there are no openers for this kind of closer up to and","    including this point, so this puts a lower bound on future searches.)","","  + If the closer at `current_position` is not a potential opener,","    remove it from the delimiter stack (since we know it can't","    be a closer either).","","  + Advance `current_position` to the next element in the stack.","","After we're done, we remove all delimiters above `stack_bottom` from the","delimiter stack."],"stylingDirectives":[[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[],[] Spec</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC3" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="3"
